# Documentation Implementation Plan

Last updated: 2026-04-22 (**D2.55 closure + D2.58 reclassification + D2.73 logged**: Art. 237/239 maturity-mismatch eligibility language now reconciled across CRR and B31 CRM specs with a three-voice reconciliation — CRR outcome-voiced *"does not qualify"* / *"shall not qualify"*, PS9/24 near-final discretionary-voiced *"may not use"*, and PS1/26 final obligation-voiced *"shall not use"* — resolving the near-final → final drafting tightening flagged in D2.55. B31 CRM spec Art. 237(1) and Art. 237(2) paragraphs now cite PS1/26 verbatim *"shall not use"* with a new change-log admonition (`resolves D2.55`) quoting the PS9/24 "may not" and pointing at the comparison-PDF strikethrough / insert mark-up at `docs/assets/comparison-of-the-final-rules.pdf` pp. 221–223; FCSM out-of-scope warning in "Methods in Scope" updated with PS1/26 Art. 239(1) *"shall not use the collateral"* verbatim. CRR CRM spec Maturity Mismatch Eligibility section now cites CRR verbatim *"does not qualify"* / *"shall not qualify"* (removing a prior paraphrase that conflated CRR and B31 wording), adds a new change-log admonition explaining the outcome-voiced → obligation-voiced recasting between CRR and PS1/26, and rewrites the Art. 239(1) FCSM exclusion section to lead with CRR verbatim and then cite PS1/26 final with the near-final *"may not use"* explicitly flagged. D2.58 closed as "invalid premise"; the genuinely missing item — CRR Art. 119(2)/(3)'s short-term national-currency preferential treatment being eliminated under PS1/26 — logged as new **D2.73**. | **D2.54 closure (earlier)**: SCRA Art. 121(1) disclosure barring ladder now documented across `docs/specifications/basel31/sa-risk-weights.md` (new `### SCRA Disclosure Barring Rules (Art. 121(1)(a), (1)(b))` subsection), `docs/framework-comparison/key-differences.md`, `docs/user-guide/regulatory/basel31.md`, and `docs/user-guide/exposure-classes/institution.md`. PDF verified verbatim against `docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` p. 42. Coverage distinguishes the two asymmetric disclosure tests: (1)(a) tests requirements **and** buffers with a Grade A *ceiling* ("may not be classified as Grade A"); (1)(b) tests requirements alone with a forced Grade C ("shall be classified as Grade C"). A firm disclosing requirements but withholding buffers lands at Grade B — the prior "undisclosed → Grade C" heuristic was incorrect under final PS1/26. Near-final → final drafting-direction reversal called out explicitly (PS9/24 "Grade B floor" → PS1/26 "Grade A ceiling"). Spec also fixes three citation errors in the SCRA table (Grade A row was citing the non-existent Art. 121(2)(b); now Art. 121(1)(a); Grade B and Grade C rows now cite Art. 121(1)(b) and (1)(c) explicitly). Coverage spans the full PRA PS1/26 Art. 124D text from `docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` pp. 52–53: (1) Art. 124D(1) scope quote (regulatory RE only, SA only); (2) Art. 124D(8) Valuation Standard table with the four joint conditions (independent valuer **or** suitably robust statistical method; no speculative uplift; market-value cap; purchase-price cap) plus info admonition positioning the statistical-method route as a peer of independent valuer; (3) Art. 124D(2) monitoring obligation (frequent market-value monitoring, more frequent in stressed markets — upstream of the calculator); (4) Art. 124D(3) definition of "qualifying valuation" as the anchor for Art. 124C LTV denominator / Art. 124F–I tables / Art. 124J floor, with the "subject to paragraph 9" self-build carve-out; (5) Art. 124D(4)–(5) revaluation trigger table covering origination (4); event-driven permanent impairment (5)(a); market-driven decline >10% (5)(b); loans >GBP 2.6m or 5% own funds after 3 years (5)(c); 5-year staleness (5)(d) — with an explicit warning admonition that the GBP 2.6m threshold applies to **all regulatory RE** not just CRE (the "not just CRE" point was the explicit D2.43 finding) and a CRR-comparison info admonition noting legacy CRR Art. 208(3)'s 1-year CRE / 3-year RRE split that Art. 124D flattens; (6) Art. 124D(6) optional revaluation for unequivocal value-increasing modifications; (7) Art. 124D(7) clock-reset optionality after a (5)(b) market-decline revaluation; (8) Art. 124D(9)–(10) self-build formulas (origination: higher of pre-construction land value and 0.8 × latest qualifying valuation; post-revaluation variants (10)(a) without land estimate and (10)(b) with) with an explicit warning that CRR had no self-build provision — Art. 124D(9)–(10) is new regulatory drafting; (9) Art. 124D(11) transitional rule for pre-2027 exposures verbatim plus a table mapping (11)(b)(i)/(ii)/(iii) escape hatches with an info admonition on residual Art. 124D(8) quality conditions; (10) Implementation Status warning clarifying firm-side governance responsibility — the calculator consumes `re_split_property_value` as an already-qualifying input, with no fields for valuation source, revaluation date, or self-build flag; (11) CRR Comparison section pointing to legacy Art. 125/126/208(3)/229 and summarising the five new Basel 3.1 elements. Docs build validated — no errors, no warnings. Last remaining P1 open item closed.

- [x] **D1.49** — ~~**Project-wide LFSE article citation and threshold precision inconsistent with PS1/26 Glossary.**~~ **FIXED (2026-04-21):** PDF verification confirmed: (1) CRR Art. 142(1)(4) pp. 137–138 defines "large financial sector entity" with the **EUR 70 billion** total-assets threshold; (2) PS1/26 Glossary p. 78 redefines it at **GBP 79 billion** (exact, not an FX conversion) with Note "corresponds to Article 142(1)(4) of CRR as it applied immediately before revocation by the Treasury"; (3) CRR Art. 4(1)(146) is the "large institution" definition (G-SII / O-SII), entirely unrelated to LFSEs — the prior cross-doc citation was wrong. All 13 affected doc files corrected: `framework-comparison/key-differences.md` (section rewritten: added framework-split LFSE threshold table, GBP 79bn exact-value info admonition, corrected Art. 147A(1)(d)→(1)(e) typo); `framework-comparison/technical-reference.md` (LFSE bullet list replaced with framework-split table, BCBS USD 100bn carve-out preserved, new code-divergence warning admonition for the unimplemented B31 GBP 79bn threshold); `appendix/glossary.md` (FI Scalar entry now dual-cites CRR Art. 142(1)(4) + PS1/26 Glossary p. 78); `user-guide/methodology/irb-approach.md` (FSE correlation section split by framework); `user-guide/regulatory/basel31.md` (LFSE defined as GBP 79bn under B31 with CRR EUR 70bn equivalent noted); `data-model/input-schemas.md` (`total_assets` field comment + FSE section with framework-split citation table); `specifications/basel31/model-permissions.md` (5 occurrences: front-matter citation, two distinct-thresholds admonitions, FSE definition paragraph, B31-M3/M3a scenario rows — all now cite PS1/26 Glossary with CRR Art. 142(1)(4) Note); `specifications/basel31/firb-calculation.md` (2 occurrences: FSE definition note, FI Scalar paragraph); `specifications/crr/firb-calculation.md` (3 occurrences: FSE definition note, FI Scalar heading, distinct-thresholds admonition); `specifications/crr/airb-calculation.md` (2 occurrences: FI Scalar paragraph, approach-restriction distinction admonition); `specifications/crr/slotting-approach.md` (Large FSE Threshold section with framework split); `specifications/index.md` + `specifications/basel31/index.md` (model-permissions row refs); `architecture/data-flow.md` + `architecture/components.md` (code comments updated). Also corrected incidental Art. 147A typo (`147A(1)(d)` → `147A(1)(e)`) in key-differences.md and airb-calculation.md — Art. 147A(1)(d) covers OF/PF/CF specialised lending; (1)(e) is the correct letter for large-corporate / FSE F-IRB restriction per PS1/26 Art. 147A. Docs build validated — no errors, no warnings. New code-side finding logged as **D3.58** (config.py:586 and line 600 docstring still carry "Art. 4(1)(146)"; B31 `lfse_total_assets_threshold` is hardcoded to `Decimal("0")` rather than GBP 79 billion, so the threshold exists nowhere in code — implementation relies entirely on the upstream `apply_fi_scalar` flag).

- [x] **D2.37** — ~~**Model permissions: retail "A-IRB only" misleadingly implies new B31 restriction.**~~ **FIXED (2026-04-21):** PDF verification against `docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` pp. 88, 91–92 and `docs/assets/crr.pdf` (original CRR Art. 151) confirmed: (a) the current spec table row uses Art. 147A(1)(**g**) — the letter (the original D2.37 finding's Art. 147A(1)(f) reference was stale, pre-dating the D4.91 letter-mapping correction — (f) now covers other general corporates per Art. 147(2)(c)(iii), (g) covers retail per Art. 147(2)(d)); (b) **retail → A-IRB-only is a CRR carry-forward, not a new B31 restriction** — CRR Art. 151(7) already required firms applying IRB to retail to "provide own estimates of LGDs and conversion factors" (i.e. A-IRB), and CRR Art. 151(8) restricted F-IRB (supervisory LGDs under Art. 161(1), supervisory CCFs under Art. 166(8)(a)–(d)) to exposure classes (a)–(c) only, explicitly omitting retail; (c) the M=1 maturity parameter for retail is Art. 154(1)(c), not Art. 147A(1)(f)/(g) — a separate IRB-formula property, not an approach restriction. CRR Art. 151(7)`; new `!!! info "Retail A-IRB-Only Is a CRR Carry-Forward, Not a New B31 Restriction"` admonition inserted after the "Earlier drafts incorrectly cited Art. 147A(1)(d)" note, with verbatim CRR Art. 151(7)/151(8) reasoning, a three-bullet list of what the B31 retail changes **actually** are (PD/LGD/EAD input floors per Art. 160/164(4)/166, QRRE transactor/non-transactor split and £90k single-obligor threshold per Art. 147(5A)(c), M=1 under Art. 154(1)(c) unchanged), and a cross-link to the CRR/B31 approach matrix in `framework-comparison/key-differences.md#irb-approach-restrictions`. - [x] **D2.39** — ~~**CRM: Art. 237–238 maturity mismatch applicability to guarantees not explicitly confirmed.**~~ **FIXED (2026-04-21):** PDF verified verbatim against `docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` pp. 217–219 (PS1/26 Section 5 — Maturity Mismatches). Original finding under-scoped: the issue is not just guarantee applicability but heading + scope + formula attribution. Verbatim findings: (1) **Art. 238(1A)** enumerates exactly six methods in scope — (a) on-balance sheet netting, (b) FCCM (excl. SFTs with master netting agreement), (c) FCM, (d) Other Funded Credit Protection Method, (e) RWSM, (f) PSM. Methods (a)–(d) are funded; (e)–(f) are unfunded. (2) **Art. 237** sets the eligibility gates that govern *all six* methods (Art. 237(A1) refers explicitly to "the methods set out in paragraph 1A of Article 238"). (3) **Art. 239** holds the formulas: paragraph 2 contains the funded `CVAM = CVA × (t − 0.25)/(T − 0.25)` for methods (a)–(d); paragraph 3 contains the unfunded `GA = G* × (t − 0.25)/(T − 0.25)` for methods (e)–(f); paragraph 1 *excludes* FCSM. The earlier B31 spec heading "Maturity Mismatch (Art. 237-238)" therefore (i) cited the wrong article for the formula (formula is Art. 239, not Art. 238) and (ii) showed only the unfunded GA branch with no explicit funded CVAM branch and no scope statement. (4) **LGD-AM (Art. 183)** is the only unfunded-protection mechanism *outside* the Art. 237–239 perimeter — not in Art. 238(1A); maturity mismatches captured inside the institution's own LGD model. Fix applied across 3 files: (1) **`docs/specifications/basel31/credit-risk-mitigation.md`** — `## Maturity Mismatch (Art. 237-238)` section (old lines 425–453) rewritten as `## Maturity Mismatch (Art. 237-239)` with five new subsections: (a) PS1/26 page-pinned scope statement; (b) "Methods in Scope (Art. 238(1A))" 6-row table tagging each method as Funded/Unfunded; (c) `!!! warning "FCSM and LGD-AM are out of scope"` admonition cross-linking to the existing `### Art. 222 — No Maturity Mismatch` anchor; (d) "Art. 237 — Eligibility Gates" splitting Art. 237(1) (combined < 3m residual + shorter-than-exposure test) from Art. 237(2) (original maturity < 1y limb (a) and Art. 162(3) one-day M-floor limb (b)); (e) "Art. 238 — Measuring Protection Maturity" with the protection-seller / protection-buyer / grace-period rules verbatim; (f) "Art. 239 — Adjustment Formulas (Funded vs Unfunded)" with both `CVAM` and `GA` formulas side-by-side, identical multipliers, different inputs; closing `!!! info "Heading scope correction (21 April 2026)"` admonition recording the fix and citing D2.39. (2) **`docs/specifications/crr/credit-risk-mitigation.md`** — old separate `## Maturity Mismatch Eligibility (CRR Art. 237)` and `## Maturity Mismatch Adjustment (CRR Art. 238)` sections replaced with a single `## Maturity Mismatch (CRR Art. 237-239)` umbrella section + retained subsections; new `### Methods in Scope (CRR Art. 238(1A))` 6-row table; eligibility section restructured into three numbered limbs covering Art. 237(1) combined test, Art. 237(2)(a), Art. 237(2)(b); adjustment section relabelled `## Maturity Mismatch Adjustment (CRR Art. 239)` and showing both `CVAM` (funded) and `GA` (unfunded) formulas with B31-alignment cross-link `../basel31/credit-risk-mitigation.md#maturity-mismatch-art-237-239`. (3) **`docs/features/index.md`** — Maturity Mismatch row updated: description widened from "CRR Art. 238 adjustment for collateral/guarantee maturity shorter than exposure" to "CRR Art. 237–239 adjustment for funded (CVAM) and unfunded (GA) protection where credit-protection maturity is shorter than the exposure"; spec link target updated from old `#maturity-mismatch-adjustment-crr-art-238` to new `#maturity-mismatch-adjustment-crr-art-239` to match the renamed CRR heading. Docs build validated — no errors, no warnings; all anchor cross-links resolve in the built HTML. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 237–239 (ps126app1.pdf pp. 217–219)

- [x] **D2.40** — ~~**CRM: LGD-AM method scope does not note A-IRB own-LGD permission requirement.**~~ **FIXED (2026-04-21):** PDF verified verbatim against `docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` — Art. 143(2A)(c) (p.81) grants A-IRB permission per exposure class / subclass / type of exposure (not institution-wide); Art. 143(2B)(b)(iii) (p.81) requires further PRA permission to move a class from F-IRB to A-IRB; Art. 179(1)(aa) (p.131) is the prohibition that "an institution shall **not** take account of recoveries from guarantees, credit derivatives and other support arrangements when quantifying LGD estimates, **except where recoveries are recognised under the LGD Adjustment Method in accordance with Article 183**"; Art. 183 (pp.139–140) is the LGD-AM requirements article; Art. 147A (p.92) removes A-IRB entirely from sovereigns/quasi-sovereigns (Art. 147A(1)(a)), institutions (Art. 147A(1)(b)), large corporates and FSEs (Art. 147A(1)(e)), and equities (Art. 147A(1)(d)); Art. 191A(3) is the portfolio-wide consistency rule requiring same method across same type of unfunded protection. Fix touched 4 files: (1) `docs/specifications/basel31/credit-risk-mitigation.md` — Method Names table row for LGD-AM scope column extended from "A-IRB: unfunded credit protection (Art. 183)" to "A-IRB **with own-LGD estimate permission** for the exposure class: unfunded credit protection (Art. 183)"; Art. 191A Part 3 decision tree split the collapsed "F-IRB / A-IRB" line into three explicit lines (F-IRB → PSM only; A-IRB without own-LGD for class → PSM only; A-IRB with own-LGD → LGD-AM or PSM by firm methodology choice under Art. 191A(3)); Method Selection by Approach table split the A-IRB row into two rows keyed on own-LGD permission; new `!!! warning "LGD-AM is not universally available to A-IRB firms"` admonition directly under the table with cross-link to the new availability-gate section; new subsection `### LGD-AM Availability Gate (Art. 143, Art. 179(1)(aa), Art. 147A)` inserted before the FCSM section covering four gating provisions — (a) Art. 143(2A)(c) class-level permission with Art. 143(2B)(b)(iii) upgrade-path note, (b) Art. 179(1)(aa) verbatim quote establishing LGD-AM as the *only* channel for guarantee recognition inside own-LGD, (c) Art. 147A restriction table enumerating the four limbs that remove A-IRB from the menu for sovereigns/quasi-sovereigns, institutions, large corporates/FSEs, and equities, (d) Art. 191A(3) portfolio consistency rule, plus a closing `!!! info "Decision summary — where LGD-AM is available"` admonition listing the four cumulative conditions. - [x] **D2.43** — ~~**Art. 124D valuation requirements not documented.** Key missing provisions: (a) loans >GBP 2.6m (or 5% of own funds) require independent valuer revaluation every 3 years for all regulatory RE (not just CRE); (b) self-build valuation = max(land value at origination, qualifying valuation × 0.8); (c) transitional rule for pre-2027 exposures. *(Phase 8 correction: threshold was incorrectly stated as GBP 2.5m; PDF Art. 124D(5)(c) confirms GBP 2.6m. ### New Phase 8 Findings — Comparison PDF (PS9/24 Near-Final → PS1/26 Final)

- [x] **D2.54** — ~~**SCRA Grade A: Art. 121(1)(a) non-disclosure consequence strengthened in final PS1/26.**~~ **FIXED (2026-04-22):** PDF verified verbatim against `docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` p. 42 (PS1/26 Art. 121(1) — three sub-paragraphs (a)/(b)/(c)). The final rule contains **two distinct disclosure barring tests**, not one: (1)(a) *"If such minimum financial regulatory requirements **and buffers** (other than institution-specific minimum requirements or buffers) are not publicly disclosed or otherwise made available by the counterparty institution, the counterparty institution **may not be classified as Grade A**"*; (1)(b) *"If such minimum financial regulatory requirements are not publicly disclosed or otherwise made available by the counterparty institution, the counterparty institution **shall be classified as Grade C**"*. The asymmetry — (1)(a) tests **requirements + buffers** with a Grade A ceiling, (1)(b) tests **requirements alone** with a forced Grade C — means a firm that discloses requirements but withholds buffers lands at **Grade B at best**, not Grade C. Prior docs captured only the (1)(b) "undisclosed → Grade C" rule. Fix applied to 4 files: (1) `docs/specifications/basel31/sa-risk-weights.md` — new `### SCRA Disclosure Barring Rules (Art. 121(1)(a), (1)(b))` subsection inserted after the "Grade A vs Grade A Enhanced" admonition and before "SCRA Short-Term Trade Finance Exception (Art. 121(4))"; coverage includes the 3-row barring-ladder table, verbatim Art. 121(1)(a)/(1)(b) quote admonitions, institution-specific carve-out (confidential Pillar 2 add-on excluded), Art. 121(1A) CRR-firm disclosure-scope enumeration (Required Level of Own Funds, regulation 34(1), leverage ratio minimum, combined buffer, countercyclical leverage buffer, additional leverage buffer), Art. 121(1B) third-country local-equivalent extension, near-final → final drafting-direction reversal warning (PS9/24 "shall not be classified as Grade B or lower" → PS1/26 "may not be classified as Grade A" — opposite outcomes), and implementation-status note confirming `scra_grade` is a firm-supplied input with no audit column surfacing the barring-rule outcome. Additionally corrected three citation errors in the same spec: Grade A row was citing "Art. 121(2)(b)" (does not exist — paragraph 2 is Table 5 RWs only) → corrected to Art. 121(1)(a); Grade B and Grade C rows now cite Art. 121(1)(b) and Art. 121(1)(c) explicitly to match the key-differences.md pattern. - [x] **D2.55** — ~~**Art. 237/239 maturity mismatch exclusion made mandatory ("shall not") in final PS1/26.** Near-final Art. 237(1) said "may not use that protection" (discretionary); final says "shall not use that protection" (mandatory). Same change in Art. 239(1) for FCSM. CRR CRM spec (`crr/credit-risk-mitigation.md` line 496) says "may not be used" — matches near-final, not final. PDF verified verbatim against (a) PS1/26 final: `docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` pp. 217–219 (Art. 237(1) *"an institution **shall not use** that protection as eligible credit protection"*; Art. 237(2) chapeau *"an institution **shall not use** the credit protection as eligible credit protection where either..."*; Art. 239(1) *"an institution using the Financial Collateral Simple Method **shall not use** the collateral as eligible funded credit protection"*); (b) near-final vs final comparison document: `docs/assets/comparison-of-the-final-rules.pdf` pp. 221–223 — strikethrough / insert mark-up shows the exact `"may" → "shall"` deltas in all three paragraphs (`"an institution mayshall not use"`); (c) CRR legacy: `docs/assets/crr.pdf` pp. 232–233 which uses outcome-voiced *"that protection does not qualify as eligible credit protection"* (Art. 237(1)), *"the credit protection shall not qualify as eligible"* (Art. 237(2)), *"the collateral does not qualify as eligible funded credit protection"* (Art. 239(1)). - [ ] **D2.56** — **Art. 124E(5) mandatory reassessment obligation not documented.** Final PS1/26 requires institutions to "reassess" (not merely "assess") whether a residential RE exposure is materially cash-flow dependent whenever a new loan is issued on the same property or replacing an existing loan to the same obligor. Commercial RE must be reassessed at least annually (Art. 124E(7)). Both requirements absent from all specs and user guides. Distinct from D1.41 (three-property limit for IPRE classification). **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 124E(5)/(7)

- [ ] **D2.57** — **CRR Art. 120(2) Table 4 short-term institution preferential treatment absent from CRR calculator branch.** `sa/calculator.py` CRR branch (lines 914–1094) has no check for rated institution exposures with residual maturity ≤3 months. Per CRR Art. 120(2) Table 4: CQS 1–3 = 20%, CQS 4–5 = 50%, CQS 6 = 150%. Without this, CQS 4–5 short-term institutions receive 100% (double the required 50%). B31 branch correctly implements ECRA short-term at lines 726–748. CRR branch has an analogous PSE short-term check (line 996–1002) but no institution equivalent. Spec `crr/sa-risk-weights.md` (lines 219–228) documents Table 4 correctly — the gap is code-only. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 120(2), IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN cross-ref needed

- [~] **D2.58** — ~~**Art. 119(3) third-country institution equivalence condition not documented.**~~ **RECLASSIFIED (2026-04-22):** PDF verification against `docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` p. 40 shows **PS1/26 Art. 119(3) is `[Note: Provision left blank]`** — not a third-country equivalence rule. The Phase 8 finding description was wrong. PS1/26 Art. 119 collapses CRR's Art. 119(1)–(6) down to just (1) rated → Art. 120 and (1A) unrated → Art. 121; paragraphs (2), (3), (4) are each marked blank and (5), (6) are "not in PRA Rulebook". There is no institution-specific third-country equivalence paragraph in PS1/26 Art. 119 at all — the closest analogue is Art. 114(7) for **sovereigns** (domestic-currency RW assignment by equivalent third-country competent authorities, which does not extend to institutions). The actual change between CRR and PS1/26 in this area is the **elimination of CRR Art. 119(2)/(3)'s short-term national-currency preferential treatment** (CRR allowed ≤ 3-month national-currency institution exposures to get sovereign-derived RW floored at 20%; PS1/26 blanks these paragraphs, so all short-term institution exposures flow through Art. 120(2) Table 4 or Art. 121(3)). This actual change is logged as a new follow-up below (D2.73). D2.58 itself is closed as "invalid premise".

- [ ] **D2.73** — **CRR Art. 119(2)/(3) short-term national-currency preferential treatment blanked in PS1/26 — removal not documented.** PDF verified: CRR Art. 119(2)–(3) (`docs/assets/crr.pdf` p. 118) allowed exposures to institutions with residual maturity ≤ 3 months, denominated and funded in the national currency of the borrower, to receive a risk weight "one category less favourable than the preferential risk weight, as described in Article 114(4) to (7), assigned to exposures to the central government in which the institution is incorporated" — with a 20% floor. PS1/26 Art. 119(2)/(3) (`docs/assets/ps126app1.pdf` p. 40) are both `[Note: Provision left blank]`, so this short-term national-currency preferential path is removed under Basel 3.1. All short-term institution exposures now flow through Art. 120(2) Table 4 (rated) or Art. 121(3) (unrated 20%). Gap: this removal is not flagged in `key-differences.md`, `technical-reference.md`, or the user-guide institution page — affects UK banks with sterling-denominated short-term exposures to institutions incorporated in jurisdictions with preferential sovereign RW (Art. 114(4)–(7)). Low impact under PRA because UK sovereign gets 0% only; primary impact is on cross-border exposures where the branch/subsidiary is incorporated in a jurisdiction that UK treasury has determined equivalent under Art. 114(7). **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 119(2)/(3) (pre-revocation) vs PS1/26 Art. 119(2)/(3) blank

## Priority 3: Code-Docs Alignment (mismatches between docs and source)

### Code Correct, Docs Wrong

- [ ] **D3.1** — `formulas.py` line 62-63 docstring: retail mortgage PD floor = 0.05%, QRRE transactors PD floor = 0.03%. Correct values: **0.10%** and **0.05%** respectively. Code and all other docs correctly use the right values.
- [x] **D3.2** — ~~`config.py` line 125: `subordinated_unsecured = 0.50` as "conservative fallback" contradicts `airb-calculation.md` correction note that 25% applies to all corporate unsecured. The `technical-reference.md` table still shows 50%.~~ **DOCS SIDE FIXED:** Investigation found `technical-reference.md` was already corrected by D1.5 (shows flat 25%, no subordinated distinction, explicit correction admonition). The remaining issue is `api/configuration.md` which documented the 50% as a "conservative fallback" without flagging it as a code divergence. Updated: (1) warning admonition rewritten to clearly state `subordinated_unsecured = 0.50` has **no regulatory basis** under Art. 161(5)(a) and should be `0.25`; (2) impact documented: subordinated exposures receive 50% floor instead of correct 25% when `exposure_class` column is unavailable (`formulas.py:164,220`); (3) inline code comment changed from "Conservative fallback (see note)" to "WRONG: should be 0.25 (see warning)". Normal pipeline path (with `exposure_class` present) correctly applies 25% regardless of seniority. **Code fix still needed:** `config.py:126,206` `subordinated_unsecured` should be changed from `Decimal("0.50")` to `Decimal("0.25")`, or the field removed entirely since `get_floor()` already routes all corporate unsecured to `self.unsecured` (25%). ### New Phase 3 Code-Docs Findings

- [ ] **D3.11** — Equity calculator docstring (`equity/calculator.py:21`): "CIU fallback: 150% → 250%". Both values wrong — Art. 132(2) fallback is **1,250%** for both CRR2 and PRA PS1/26. The 250% is Art. 133 equity weight, not CIU fallback. See D3.15 for the underlying code bug.
- [ ] **D3.12** — CRR HIGH_RISK exposure class treated as active in CRR engine path (`sa/calculator.py:1041-1045`). If Art. 128 is omitted from UK law (see D1.28), these exposures should fall through to Art. 133 (equity 100%) or their counterparty's standard class treatment, not 150%. Basel 3.1 path (`sa/calculator.py:859`) is correct (Art. 128 re-introduced). Cross-reference D1.28 — needs verification of whether PRA Rulebook (CRR Firms) retains an Art. 128 equivalent.
- [ ] **D3.13** — `b31_risk_weights.py` module docstring (line 16): says "CQS5: 100%". Line 327 docstring: says "CQS5=100%". Both wrong — PRA retains CQS 5 = **150%**. The code constant itself is correct (`5: Decimal("1.50")` at line 143). Docstrings only.
- [ ] **D3.14** — `b31_risk_weights.py` `B31_ECRA_SHORT_TERM_RISK_WEIGHTS` (lines 197-204): CQS 4 and CQS 5 both set to `Decimal("0.20")` (20%). PRA PS1/26 Art. 120(2) Table 4 confirms CQS 4-5 = **50%**. Code comment at line 189 ("CQS 1-5 all receive 20%") also wrong. Only CQS 1-3 receive 20%; CQS 4-5 receive 50%. Discovered during D1.22 fix — verified against PDF extraction.
- [ ] **D3.15** — CIU fallback risk weight code bug: Art. 132(2) specifies **1,250%** for both CRR2 and PRA PS1/26. Code uses 150% CRR (`crr_equity_rw.py:48`, `CIU: Decimal("1.50")`), 250% B31 listed / 400% B31 unlisted (`b31_equity_rw.py:49`, `equity/calculator.py:577-582`). These values correspond to **Art. 133 equity SA weights**, not the Art. 132(2) CIU fallback. The calculator's `ciu_approach = "fallback"` pathway should apply 1,250% per regulation. The 250%/400% treatment belongs to CIU exposures **excluded** under Art. 132B(2) that are reclassified as standard equity. Enum docstring (`enums.py:465`) and calculator docstring (`equity/calculator.py:21`) also cite wrong values. Extends D1.20, D1.29, D3.11. Discovered via PDF cross-check of PS1/26 page 62.
- [ ] **D3.16** — `regulatory-tables.md` SA Equity table previously showed B31 values (250%/400%) under heading "SA Equity (CRR Art. 133)". CRR Art. 133(2) assigns flat 100% to all equity. Table restructured during D1.20 fix to separate CRR and B31 with code-vs-regulation columns, but the underlying code constants (`SA_EQUITY_RISK_WEIGHTS`) are CRR-correct (100% flat) except for CIU (150% instead of 1,250%).
- [ ] **D3.17** — CRR institution CQS 2 risk weight code bug: `crr_risk_weights.py` `INSTITUTION_RISK_WEIGHTS_UK` uses **30%** for CQS 2 (line 67), labelled "UK deviation". PDF verification of UK onshored CRR Art. 120 Table 3 confirms CQS 2 = **50%**. The 30% value matches **Basel 3.1 ECRA** (PRA PS1/26 Art. 120 Table 3), not CRR. No PRA Rulebook instrument or supervisory statement has been identified that overrides CRR Art. 120 Table 3 for CQS 2. Affects: `crr_risk_weights.py` (lines 64-67 constant + lines 86-105 function), `sa/calculator.py:1480` comment. The `_create_institution_df` function is also reused for Basel 3.1 ECRA (`b31_risk_weights.py` imports it with `use_uk_deviation=True`), which means B31 ECRA is correctly applying 30% — but via the wrong mechanism (CRR "UK deviation" flag rather than B31-specific table). CRR acceptance test CRR-A4 expects £300k (30% RW) — will need updating to £500k (50% RW). MDB Table 2B CQS 2 = 30% (`crr_risk_weights.py` line 229) also needs verification against CRR Art. 117. Discovered during D1.30 fix via PDF cross-check of crr.pdf page 119 and ps126app1.pdf page 40. (2026-04-09)
- [ ] **D3.18** — CRR retail payroll/pension 35% not implemented in CRR code path. `sa/calculator.py` CRR branch has no `is_payroll_loan` check — all CRR retail exposures receive flat 75%. The 35% treatment exists in CRR since CRR2 (Regulation 2019/876, Art. 123 second subparagraph). Also: code constant comment `B31_RETAIL_PAYROLL_LOAN_RW` in `b31_risk_weights.py:212` and schema comments in `schemas.py:80,101,642` cite "Art. 123(3)(a-b)" — should be **Art. 123(4)**. Art. 123(3) covers the risk weight tiers (45%/75%/100%), not payroll/pension. Discovered during D4.19 fix via PDF cross-check. (2026-04-09)
- [ ] **D3.19** — B31 defaulted provision threshold denominator code bug: `calculator.py:1250-1275` uses `unsecured_ead` (post-provision unsecured exposure value) as the Basel 3.1 provision-coverage denominator. PRA PS1/26 Art. 127(1) specifies **"the outstanding amount of the item or facility"** — the gross outstanding balance, not the unsecured portion. This underestimates the denominator for partially collateralised exposures, making it harder to reach the 20% threshold than the regulation intends. CRR path (`calculator.py:1276-1291`) correctly uses pre-provision unsecured value per CRR Art. 127(1). Discovered during D4.32 fix via PDF cross-check of crr.pdf pages 126-127 and ps126app1.pdf page 59. (2026-04-09)
- [ ] **D3.20** — Art. 114 paragraph number errors in source code comments. `calculator.py` (lines 511, 513, 603, 919, 1513), `classifier.py` (lines 906-907, 966), `eu_sovereign.py` (lines 5, 18), and `guarantee.py` (lines 188, 206) all reference "Art. 114(3)/(4)" for domestic currency treatment. Art. 114(3) is the **ECB** provision, not UK domestic currency. UK domestic = Art. 114(4); EU domestic = Art. 114(7) (third-country reciprocity in UK-onshored CRR). `classifier.py:966` specifically labels EU CGCB treatment as "Art. 114(4)" — should be Art. 114(7). Discovered during D4.35 fix via PDF cross-check of crr.pdf pp. 112-113 and ps126app1.pdf pp. 35-36. (2026-04-09)
- [ ] **D3.21** — B31 rated covered bond risk weights code bug: `b31_risk_weights.py` `B31_COVERED_BOND_RISK_WEIGHTS` (lines 261–268) uses **BCBS CRE20.28–29** values (CQS 2 = 15%, CQS 6 = 50%). PRA PS1/26 Art. 129(4) Table 7 is **identical to CRR Table 6A** — CQS 2 = **20%**, CQS 6 = **100%**. The PRA did not adopt the BCBS reductions. Affects: rated covered bond RW lookup for B31 framework only — CQS 2 (over-favourable by 5pp) and CQS 6 (over-favourable by 50pp). Unrated derivation (`COVERED_BOND_UNRATED_DERIVATION`, `B31_COVERED_BOND_UNRATED_FROM_SCRA`) is correct. Also: `b31_risk_weights.py` line 263 comment says "CRR: 20%" for CQS 2 implying a change — there is no change. Discovered during D4.20 fix via PDF cross-check of crr.pdf page 129 and ps126app1.pdf page 61. (2026-04-09)
- [ ] **D3.22** — CRR HVCRE slotting risk weight code bug: `crr_slotting.py` defines `SLOTTING_RISK_WEIGHTS_HVCRE` and `SLOTTING_RISK_WEIGHTS_HVCRE_SHORT` with EU CRR Table 2 values (Strong: 95%/70%, Good: 120%/95%, Satisfactory: 140%/140%, Weak: 250%/250%). The UK onshored CRR has **no HVCRE concept** — Art. 153(5) contains only Table 1 for all SL types. "High volatility commercial real estate" does not appear anywhere in the UK CRR text. The EU CRR Table 2 was not retained in UK onshoring. These constants have no UK CRR legal basis. The code is more conservative than required (higher RWs for `is_hvcre=True` CRR exposures). CRR acceptance tests CRR-E4, CRR-E7, CRR-E8 test HVCRE behavior using these values. PRA PS1/26 introduces HVCRE as a new sub-type in Table A — B31 HVCRE constants (`B31_SLOTTING_RISK_WEIGHTS_HVCRE`) are correct. Discovered during D4.23 fix via full-text PDF search of crr.pdf (2026-03-02 legislation.gov.uk version). (2026-04-09)

### New Phase 5 Code-Docs Findings

- [ ] **D3.23** — B31 guarantee substitution: `_apply_guarantee_substitution()` at `sa/calculator.py:1428-1709` has **zero** `is_basel_3_1` checks. Uses CRR CQS tables for both frameworks. Affects: (a) corporate CQS 3 guarantors = 100% (B31 Table 6 = 75%), (b) unrated institution guarantors use CRR sovereign-derived 40% (B31 should use SCRA grades), (c) no short-term guarantor institution treatment. This is the root cause of P1.95, P1.110, P1.122 in IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md. Docs correctly describe the B31 guarantee substitution rules; code does not implement them. **Effort: M** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 122/121/235

- [ ] **D3.24** — B31 government-supported equity 100% RW has no PRA PS1/26 basis. `b31_equity_rw.py:44` sets `GOVERNMENT_SUPPORTED: Decimal("1.00")`. The `b31/equity-approach.md` spec documents this but IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md P1.132 identifies it as a bug: PRA PS1/26 Art. 133(6) is an exclusion clause directing own-funds deduction items elsewhere, not a 100% RW category. Government-supported equity under B31 should receive 250% (standard, Art. 133(3)). Docs should add a code divergence warning. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 133(3)/(6), P1.132

### New Phase 6 Code-Docs Findings

- [ ] **D3.25** — **B31 CRE loan-split threshold "60% LTV" in `sa-risk-weights.md` should be "55% of property value".** `docs/specifications/basel31/sa-risk-weights.md` line 487 says secured portion is "up to 60% LTV". Code correctly uses `B31_COMMERCIAL_GENERAL_MAX_SECURED_RATIO = Decimal("0.55")` at `b31_risk_weights.py:112`. The `regulatory-tables.md` also correctly says "≤ 55% (secured portion)". The 60% conflates the **risk weight** with the **split threshold**. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 124H(1)

- [ ] **D3.26** — **B31 SME corporate threshold "EUR 50m" in 2 doc files should be "GBP 44m".** `regulatory-tables.md` line 107 and `key-differences.md` line 399 both cite EUR 50m as the B31 SME corporate threshold. PRA PS1/26 Art. 122(11) specifies GBP 44m. Code correctly uses `B31_SME_TURNOVER_THRESHOLD_GBP = Decimal("44000000")`. `sa-risk-weights.md` correctly says GBP 44m. Partially overlaps D2.32 but adds `regulatory-tables.md` as a second affected file. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 122(11)

- [ ] **D3.27** — **`firb_lgd.py` `get_firb_lgd_table()` is framework-agnostic — always returns CRR values.** Function has no `is_basel_3_1` parameter. Any code calling it directly will get CRR LGD values regardless of framework. The B31 equivalent (`firb_lgd.py:get_b31_firb_lgd_table()`) exists separately but the naming pattern creates confusion risk. `regulatory-tables.md` points to dict constants not DataFrame functions, reducing practical impact. **Effort: S** | Ref: Code structure

- [ ] **D3.28** — **CRR Art. 119(2)/(3) domestic-currency short-term institution treatment undocumented and unimplemented.** Art. 119(2): exposures to institutions with residual maturity ≤3m denominated/funded in domestic currency receive RW one category less favourable than sovereign preferential, floored at 20% (Art. 119(3)). Distinct from Art. 120/121 tables. In UK: sterling short-term claim on UK institution → 20% (one notch above 0% sovereign). Code has no Art. 119(2) branch. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 119(2)/(3)

- [ ] **D3.29** — **`covered_bond_unrated_derivation` in `crr_risk_weights.py` has 7 entries but CRR Art. 129(5) only produces 4.** The 3 extra entries (30%, 40%, 75% institution RW) only arise under B31 SCRA — they don't occur in CRR where unrated institutions get sovereign-derived rates (20%/50%/100%). Comment says "CRR Art. 129(5), PRA PS1/26 Art. 129" — misleading dual attribution. Won't produce wrong CRR results but structurally conflates frameworks. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 129(5)

### New Phase 8 Findings — Comparison PDF & COREP/Pillar III

- [ ] **D3.30** — **Art. 129(1B): new PRA permission for CQS 2 covered bond concentration not documented.** Entirely new in final PS1/26 (not in PS9/24 near-final). Allows institutions, with PRA permission, to apply CQS 2 for up to 10% of outstanding covered bonds of the issuing institution where the CQS 1 requirement (Art. 129(1)(c)) creates significant UK concentration problems. Not mentioned in `key-differences.md`, `sa-risk-weights.md`, or any other doc. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 129(1B)

- [ ] **D3.31** — **OF 09.01 multiple rows not documented.** PDF (ps1-26-annex-ii-reporting-instructions, pp. 139–141) defines rows absent from `output-reporting.md` and `reporting-differences.md`: (a) rows 0075/0085/0095 = "of which: SME" sub-rows under corporates/retail/RE; (b) rows 0141/0142/0143 = CIU sub-rows (look-through/mandate-based/fall-back); (c) row 0160 = Other items (Art. 112(1)(q)); (d) row 0170 = Total exposures. Current D3.9 "Missing Row IDs — OF 09.01" in `output-reporting.md` lists only rows 0071–0073 and 0091–0094. **Effort: M** | Ref: ps1-26-annex-ii-reporting-instructions.pdf pp. 139–141

- [ ] **D3.32** — **UKB CR6-A column structure (cols a–e) entirely absent from disclosure docs.** `disclosure-differences.md` notes row changes (exposure classes → roll-out classes) but never defines the 5 columns: (a) IRB exposure value per Art. 166A–166D, (b) total exposure value (SA+IRB), (c) % subject to PPU SA, (d) % subject to IRB, (e) % subject to roll-out plan. CRR version had same column labels but different definitions. **Effort: S** | Ref: Annex XXII (Pillar III instructions) pp. 7–9

- [ ] **D3.33** — **UKB CR9 backtesting template column definitions (a–h) not documented.** Neither `output-reporting.md` nor `disclosure-differences.md` documents these columns. Key definitions: col (a) PD range (pre-floor for bucket assignment), cols (c/d) number of obligors/defaulted, col (f) EWA PD (post-input-floor), col (g) average PD at disclosure date, col (h) average historical annual default rate (5-year average). **Effort: S** | Ref: Annex XXII pp. 18–22

- [ ] **D3.34** — **CMS1/CMS2 reference PDF missing from `docs/assets/`.** `output-reporting.md` (line 197) references `ps1-26-annex-ii-output-floor-and-capital-summaries-disclosure-instructions.pdf` as source for CMS1/CMS2 templates, but this file does not exist in `docs/assets/`. Templates are marked "Done" in status section (line 201) despite missing instruction source. Either add the PDF or correct the reference. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Annex II

- [ ] **D3.35** — **Art. 147B roll-out class enumeration not documented anywhere.** Multiple reporting/disclosure spec files (`corep-reporting.md`, `reporting-differences.md`, `disclosure-differences.md`, `output-reporting.md`, `pillar3-disclosures.md`) reference roll-out classes (Art. 147B) as the basis for OF 08.07 and UKB CR6-A rows, but no file enumerates the actual class definitions, how many there are, or their mapping to Art. 147(2) exposure classes. Implementers have no reference for which roll-out class a given exposure belongs to. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 147B

- [ ] **D3.36** — **CRR Art. 126 CRE implemented as binary whole-loan; regulation requires proportion-based split.** `crr_risk_weights.py` `calculate_commercial_re_rw()` and `calculator.py` lines 984–997 apply 50% if LTV ≤ 50% with income cover, 100% otherwise. Art. 126(2)(d) requires: 50% on the part of the loan not exceeding 50% of MV (or 60% of MLV), counterparty RW on the excess — analogous to Art. 125 RRE split which IS correctly implemented as a weighted blend. For LTV ≤ 50% the result is identical (whole loan within secured portion), but for LTV > 50% with qualifying conditions met, the code over-assigns risk. Should mirror Art. 125 pattern: `secured_share = min(1.0, 0.50 / LTV); avg_RW = 0.50 × secured_share + counterparty_RW × (1 - secured_share)`. Docs side fixed by D1.36. **Effort: S** | Ref: UK CRR Art. 126(2)(d)

- [ ] **D3.38** — **CRR Art. 164(4) portfolio-level LGD floors not implemented.** `LGDFloors.crr()` returns all zeros, but CRR Art. 164(4) (as amended by CRR2, Reg 2019/876) imposes portfolio-level minimum LGD requirements: exposure-weighted average LGD ≥ 10% for retail residential RE, ≥ 15% for retail commercial RE. These are portfolio-level (not per-exposure) floors requiring a post-aggregation validation step. The per-exposure architecture cannot directly enforce them. Docs side fixed by D1.39. **Effort: M** | Ref: UK CRR Art. 164(4)

- [ ] **D3.39** — **CRR MDB risk weight table uses Basel 3.1 Table 2B values.** `crr_risk_weights.py` defines `MDB_RISK_WEIGHTS_TABLE_2B` (lines 231-246) with CQS 2 = 30% and unrated = 50%. CRR Art. 117(1) treats non-0% MDBs "in the same manner as exposures to institutions" — they should use institution Table 3 (CQS 2 = 50% under CRR). The 30% value is the PRA PS1/26 Art. 117(1)(a) Table 2B value, not CRR. Fix: under CRR framework, route non-named MDBs to institution risk weight lookup instead of a separate MDB table; under Basel 3.1, Table 2B is correct. Related: D1.30 (same CQS 2 = 30% misattribution pattern), D3.17 (institution CQS 2 code bug). Docs side fixed by D1.40. **Effort: M** | Ref: CRR Art. 117(1), PRA PS1/26 Art. 117(1)(a)

- [ ] **D3.37** — **PE/VC always mapped to 400% higher-risk in equity calculator; regulation requires unlisted + business < 5yr test.** `equity/calculator.py` lines 570–574 assign 400% to all `private_equity` and `private_equity_diversified` equity types unconditionally. Line 570 comment: "PE/VC is always higher risk (400%)". PRA PS1/26 Glossary (p.5) defines higher-risk equity as unlisted + business has existed for less than five years. Long-established PE holdings (business ≥ 5 years) should receive standard 250% (Art. 133(3)), not 400%. Also: `b31_equity_rw.py` line 9 docstring says "PE / VC / unlisted <5yr" conflating three separate concepts. Also affects `calculator.py:549-550` docstring ("PE / VC (always higher risk)"). Fix requires: (1) add `business_age_years` or `is_established` input field; (2) route PE/VC to 400% only when both conditions met; (3) update B31-L2, B31-L19 acceptance tests. Docs side fixed by D1.38. **Effort: M** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Glossary p.5, Art. 133(3)-(4)

### New Phase 18 Findings (2026-04-18) — Code-Docs Alignment

- [ ] **D3.40** — **`input-schemas.md` omits valid `scra_grade` value `"A_ENHANCED"`.** `src/rwa_calc/data/schemas.py:619` defines `VALID_SCRA_GRADES = {"A", "A_ENHANCED", "B", "C"}`. `docs/data-model/input-schemas.md:50` lists only `"A"`, `"B"`, `"C"`. Callers populating counterparty objects from the docs alone cannot discover the implemented A-enhanced bucket (Art. 121(5) quantitative thresholds CET1 ≥ 14% / leverage ≥ 5% → 30% RW). **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 121(5), Art. 121A
- [ ] **D3.41** — **`input-schemas.md` entity_type table missing 11 implemented values.** `VALID_ENTITY_TYPES` has 29 values; docs table lists ~18. Missing: `mdb_named`, `covered_bond`, `high_risk`, `high_risk_venture_capital`, `high_risk_private_equity`, `high_risk_speculative_re`, `other_cash`, `other_gold`, `other_items_in_collection`, `other_tangible`, `other_residual_lease`. Each type has distinct regulatory treatment (Art. 128 high risk, Art. 129 covered bonds, Art. 117 MDBs, Art. 134 other items). **Effort: M** | Ref: Art. 117, 128, 129, 134
- [ ] **D3.42** — **`input-schemas.md` counterparty schema table missing 7 implemented fields.** `COUNTERPARTY_SCHEMA` defines `is_natural_person` (Art. 123 retail), `is_social_housing` (Art. 123(d)), `is_financial_sector_entity` (Art. 119(5)), `borrower_income_currency`, `sovereign_cqs` (Art. 114(4)–(6)), `local_currency`, `institution_cqs` (Art. 120). None appear in `docs/data-model/input-schemas.md:38-51`. Material omission — callers cannot correctly populate counterparty objects from docs alone. **Effort: M** | Ref: Art. 114(4)–(6), 119(5), 120, 123
- [ ] **D3.43** — **`domain/enums.py` SCRAGrade.B docstring retains fabricated quantitative thresholds.** Source line 320 reads `"""CET1 > 5.5%, Leverage > 3%, meets minimum requirements → 75% RW (>3m), 50% (≤3m)"""`. D1.34 corrected the description in `docs/api/domain.md` but did not update the source enum docstring; source now contradicts corrected docs. Art. 121(1)(b) defines Grade B qualitatively ("meets minimum requirements excluding buffers"); no CET1/leverage thresholds in regulation. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 121(1)(b); related to D1.34
- [ ] **D3.44** — **`output-schemas.md` omits PMA, double-default, currency-mismatch, and Pool B output fields.** `CALCULATION_OUTPUT_SCHEMA` includes PMA fields (`post_model_adjustment_rwa`, `mortgage_rw_floor_adjustment`, `unrecognised_exposure_adjustment`, `el_pre_adjustment`, `post_model_adjustment_el`, `el_after_adjustment`), Pool B AVA fields (`ava_amount`, `other_own_funds_reductions`), double-default fields (`is_double_default_eligible`, `double_default_unfunded_protection`, `irb_lgd_double_default`), and CRM field `currency_mismatch_multiplier_applied`. None of these appear in `docs/data-model/output-schemas.md`. Consumers of the API output have no documented contract for these fields. **Effort: M** | Ref: Art. 153(5A)/154(4A)/158(6A) (PMA), Art. 159A (Pool B AVA), Art. 153(3) (double-default), Art. 228 (currency mismatch)
- [ ] **D3.45** — **C 02.00 / OF 02.00 COREP section absent from `corep-reporting.md`.** The Own Funds Requirements master template is implemented (`_generate_c_02_00()`, `COREPTemplateBundle.c_02_00`) and described in `output-reporting.md` (pp. 97–98) but has no dedicated section in `docs/features/corep-reporting.md`. Every other implemented template (02.01, 07.00, 08.01–08.07, 09.01–09.02) has its own section. C 02.00 is the most important template (it is where the output floor is actually applied). **Effort: M** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Annex II
- [ ] **D3.46** — **C 08.05 / OF 08.05 COREP PD back-testing template absent from `corep-reporting.md`.** Implemented in generator (`_generate_all_c08_05()`) and listed in `output-reporting.md` "Missing Templates" as a documentation gap. `corep-reporting.md` has sections for every other C 08.xx template (08.01, 08.02, 08.03, 08.04, 08.06, 08.07) but no section for C 08.05. Column structure (5 cols: avg PD, obligor count, of which defaulted, observed DR, historical DR) differs from Pillar III UKB CR9 (8 columns) and needs separate coverage. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Annex II
- [ ] **D3.47** — **OF 08.01 rows 0190/0200 large-corporate IG/non-IG rationale undocumented.** `corep-reporting.md` lists new rows 0190 ("Corporates without ECAI") and 0200 ("of which: investment grade") with label only. Context not explained: these rows exist specifically for output floor calculation — firms using IRB for large corporates without ECAI must report them here to enable SA comparison under Art. 122(6)–(8). The distinction between IG (65% SA weight) and non-IG (135% SA weight) is material for the floor. No cross-reference to Art. 122(6)–(8) large corporate IG split in COREP docs. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Annex II §1.2 OF 08.01, Art. 122(6)–(8)
- [ ] **D3.48** — **Art. 144 IRB minimum requirements entry conditions entirely absent.** Art. 144 (IRB minimum requirements — conditions a firm must meet before permission is granted and on an ongoing basis) has zero coverage in any spec or user-guide file. `regulatory-references.md` lists Art. 142–150 only at group level. `model-permissions.md` focuses on Art. 147A routing restrictions, not underlying Art. 144 minimum-requirements test. Missing: rating system coverage (Art. 144(1)(a)–(g)), ongoing validation (144(1)(f)), documentation standards (144(1)(g)), and Art. 144(2) notification obligation on significant model changes. Users have no reference for what "valid IRB permission" means. **Effort: M** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 144(1)(a)–(g), Art. 144(2)
- [ ] **D3.49** — **Art. 179–184 PD/LGD/EAD estimation standards entirely absent from all docs.** `regulatory-references.md` lines 77–78 list Art. 178–181 in a one-line row with no content. No specification file documents any of: Art. 179 (general estimation requirements — long-run average, conservatism margins, data length), Art. 180 (PD estimation by exposure class, including 180(1)(a)–(f) corporate methods and 180(2)(a)–(g) retail methods), Art. 181 (LGD estimation — economic downturn LGD, collateral realisation lags, incomplete recovery data), Art. 182 (EAD/CCF estimation), Art. 183 (LGD-AM requirements under A-IRB), Art. 184 (purchased receivables estimation). `irb-approach.md` lines 503–504 cross-reference these articles but provide no content. Implementers have no documentation of what the model inputs (PD, LGD, EAD) must represent. **Effort: L** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 179–184

### New Phase 3 Minor Findings

- [ ] **D4.31** — CRR Art. 125 real estate mechanism: spec simplifies RRE treatment to "35% ≤80% LTV" implying LTV bands, but Art. 125 actual mechanism is "portion not exceeding 80% of property value receives 35%" (proportion-based, not band-based). The practical outcome is equivalent for simple cases, but the mechanism description in `sa-risk-weights.md` and `crr.md` could mislead implementers. Minor precision issue.
- [x] **D4.32** — ~~CRR Art. 127 defaulted provision denominator: spec says "Specific provisions >= 20% of (EAD + provision_deducted)".~~ **FIXED:** PDF verification revealed both CRR and B31 denominators were documented incorrectly. (1) CRR Art. 127(1) (crr.pdf pp. 126-127): denominator is "the unsecured part of the exposure value if those specific credit risk adjustments and deductions were not applied" — the **pre-provision unsecured** value, not `EAD + provision_deducted` (though the code's implementation of `(ead + provision_deducted) × unsecured_pct` is a correct interpretation). (2) PRA PS1/26 Art. 127(1) (ps126app1.pdf p. 59): denominator is "the outstanding amount of the item or facility" — the **gross outstanding** balance (not limited to unsecured, not net of provisions). B31 docs previously said "unsecured EAD" which is wrong. Corrected across 4 files: `crr/sa-risk-weights.md` (CRR table rewritten with regulatory text, CRR Art. 127(3)-(4) RE flat 100% note added, B31 table corrected, denominator comparison warning, B31 code divergence warning D3.19), `basel31/defaulted-exposures.md` (key changes table corrected "Ambiguous"→actual CRR text, formula and denominator description rewritten, FR-10.2 updated, scenario descriptions corrected, code divergence warning), `user-guide/regulatory/basel31.md` (denominator corrected, cross-link admonition added), `framework-comparison/key-differences.md` (denominator comparison admonition added with cross-link). New code bug D3.19 filed for B31 path using wrong denominator. (2026-04-09)
- [x] **D4.33** — ~~`key-differences.md` CCF table shows separate rows for "Other Commitments <1yr" and "Other Commitments ≥1yr" both at 40%.~~ **FIXED:** as part of D2.26 fix. CCF table replaced with full 7-row Table A1 structure. Row 5 is now a single "Other Commitments" row with CRR footnote explaining the maturity split removal (50%/>1yr + 20%/≤1yr → flat 40%). (2026-04-09)
- [x] **D4.34** — ~~`crr.md` CCF table (lines 138-147): shows "Undrawn credit facilities: 20%" conflating MR (50%) and MLR (20%) categories.~~ **FIXED:** as part of D4.24 fix. (2026-04-09)
- [x] **D4.35** — ~~`central-govt-central-bank.md` Art. 114 references may use wrong paragraph numbers.~~ **FIXED:** PDF verification of CRR Art. 114 (crr.pdf pp. 112-113) and PRA PS1/26 Art. 114 (ps126app1.pdf pp. 35-36) confirmed systematic paragraph number errors. Art. 114(3) = ECB → 0% (not UK domestic currency); Art. 114(4) = UK central government + Bank of England in sterling → 0% (not EU domestic currency); Art. 114(7) = third-country domestic currency reciprocity (EU member states post-Brexit). Corrected across 3 doc files: (1) `central-govt-central-bank.md` — UK section heading and code comment corrected from Art. 114(3) to Art. 114(4); EU section heading and code comment corrected from Art. 114(4) to Art. 114(7) with warning admonition explaining UK-onshored CRR narrowing of Art. 114(4) and third-country reciprocity basis; new ECB Treatment section added (Art. 114(3)); Central Bank Exposures table expanded with regulatory basis column and Art. 114(2A) admonition (PS1/26: unrated central banks use sovereign ECAI); regulatory references table restructured from 5 to 7 rows distinguishing ECB (Art. 114(3)), UK domestic (Art. 114(4)), third-country (Art. 114(7)), and central bank (Art. 114/Art. 114(2A)). (2) `changelog.md` — three historical entries corrected: v0.1.44 Art. 114(4)→Art. 114(7) for EU with correction admonition; v0.1.42 Art. 114(3)→Art. 114(4) for UK guarantor with inline correction note; v0.1.41 Art. 114(3)→Art. 114(4) for UK with correction admonition. (3) `crr/sa-risk-weights.md` — domestic currency description rewritten from generic "of that sovereign" to specific UK (Art. 114(4)), third-country (Art. 114(7)), and ECB (Art. 114(3)) provisions. Code comments in source (`calculator.py`, `classifier.py`, `eu_sovereign.py`, `guarantee.py`) also use wrong Art. 114 paragraph numbers — filed as D3.20. (2026-04-09)

### New Phase 5 Minor Findings (2026-04-10)

- [ ] **D4.37** — CRR Art. 137 ECA mapping in `crr/sa-risk-weights.md` (lines 744–750) collapses 8 MEIP values (0–7) into 5 grouped rows and maps via CQS as intermediate step. Art. 137 Table 9 has 8 separate MEIP rows mapping directly to risk weights (not CQS steps). The numerical outcome is equivalent for sovereigns but the mechanism description is a simplification. Column heading should reference MEIP (minimum export insurance premium) scores, not "ECA Risk Score". **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 137 Table 9

- [ ] **D4.38** — User guide maturity mismatch formula in `crr.md` (line 237–239) defines T without the 5-year cap. Art. 238 specifies `T = min(residual exposure maturity, 5)`. The spec file `crr/credit-risk-mitigation.md` (line 259) correctly includes the cap. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 238

The fix updated the main spec and technical-reference.md but missed this skill reference. Risk: agents consulting this file will give incorrect guidance. **Effort: S** — **BLOCKED: skill files sandbox-protected**

- [ ] **D4.41** — Skill CRR `slotting-and-equity.md` (lines 31–38) presents HVCRE Table 2 weights as CRR data without noting they have **no UK legal basis** (EU CRR only, not retained in UK onshoring per D4.23). **Effort: S** — **BLOCKED: skill files sandbox-protected**

No PRA instrument authorises 30% under CRR. The skill should mirror the spec's D1.30 correction. **Effort: S** — **BLOCKED: skill files sandbox-protected**

### New Phase 6 Minor Findings

- [ ] **D4.44** — **Art. 131 (items associated with particular high risk) blank under B31 not noted.** CRR Art. 131 was blanked by PS1/26 (replaced by Art. 128 reintroduction). `sa-risk-weights.md` CRR section documents Art. 128 (high risk 150%) but does not note that Art. 131 is blanked under B31. Minor completeness gap. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 131

- [ ] **D4.45** — **Art. 116(3A) third-country PSE sovereign-floor mechanism undocumented.** PS1/26 Art. 116(3A): PSEs of third countries treated under Art. 115(1) (sovereign-derived) receive a floor of 20% (institution treatment, Art. 121(3)) if the sovereign RW is 0%. No spec file documents this floor. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 116(3A)

- [ ] **D4.46** — **Art. 115(3) religious community regional/local government authority undocumented.** CRR Art. 115(3) allows religious communities constituted under public law to be treated as RGLAs for sovereign-derived treatment. Not mentioned in any spec or user guide. Edge case but regulatory completeness gap. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 115(3)

- [ ] **D4.47** — **Art. 129(6) pre-2007 covered bond grandfathering undocumented.** CRR Art. 129(6): covered bonds issued before 31 Dec 2007 not subject to Art. 129(1)/(3)/(6) eligibility requirements — grandfathered at maturity. Not mentioned in `sa-risk-weights.md` or `credit-risk-mitigation.md`. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 129(6)

- [ ] **D4.48** — **Art. 199(3) 70%/10% realisation test for physical collateral not documented.** CRR Art. 199(3): physical collateral (other than RE) only eligible if institution can demonstrate past collateral liquidation values ≥70% of appraised value for ≥10% of exposures. No spec mentions this eligibility test. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 199(3)

- [ ] **D4.49** — **Art. 227(4) 4-business-day close-out window for FCSM repo not documented.** CRR Art. 227(4): Financial Collateral Simple Method for repo-style transactions requires 4-business-day close-out period. Not mentioned in `credit-risk-mitigation.md` or CRM spec files. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 227(4)

- [ ] **D4.50** — **`output-floor.md` OF-ADJ formula table omits T2 cap.** The output floor adjustment formula in `output-floor.md` defines OF-ADJ = max(0, SA-RWA × OF% − IRB-RWA) but does not note the T2 capital deduction cap (the lesser of OF-ADJ and the T2 deduction per Art. 92(3)(c)). **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 92(3)

- [ ] **D4.51** — **Art. 40 supervisory deductions from CET1 unexplained in docs.** Art. 40 (prudential filters/supervisory deductions) referenced in `output-floor.md` for RWA cap calculation but not explained. Context: supervisory deductions reduce the denominator in OF-ADJ calculations. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 40

- [ ] **D4.52** — **IRB equities/CIU transition period is 3 years (2027-2029), not 4.** `equity-approach.md` correctly shows 4-year equity SA transitional (2027-2030) but the IRB equity/CIU opt-out transitional (Rules 4.5-4.10) runs only 3 years (1 Jan 2027 to 31 Dec 2029). No doc file distinguishes the two timelines. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Rules 4.5-4.10

- [ ] **D4.53** — **Table B HVCRE EL Strong subgrade A = 0.4% not documented.** `slotting-approach.md` B31 HVCRE table shows Strong EL = 0.4% without distinguishing subgrade A (0.4%) from the general Strong row. PRA PS1/26 Art. 153(5) Table B has Strong A = 0.4%, Strong = 0.8%. Code correctly handles subgrades but docs do not surface this split. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 153(5) Table B

- [ ] **D4.54** — **Art. 222(4) FCSM 10% non-core repo floor undocumented.** CRR Art. 222(4): under Financial Collateral Simple Method, repo-style transactions in non-core-market government debt receive a minimum haircut floor of 10%. Not mentioned in CRM docs. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 222(4)

- [ ] **D4.55** — **CRR Art. 121(4) trade finance short-term preferential 50%/20% undocumented.** CRR Art. 121(4): trade finance items with residual maturity ≤1 year may receive 50% (sovereign CQS 4-5) or 20% (sovereign CQS 1-3) under sovereign-derived approach. Not documented in `sa-risk-weights.md` CRR institution section or `institution.md`. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 121(4)

- [ ] **D4.56** — **Art. 118 UK exit item (f) deletion not noted.** CRR Art. 118 (exposures to recognised exchanges) — item (f) referencing EU-regulated exchanges was deleted on UK exit (SI 2018/1401). Docs reference Art. 118 without noting this deletion. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 118, SI 2018/1401

- [ ] **D4.57** — **Vehicle financing arrangement definition (Art. 4(1)(153A)) undocumented.** PS1/26 introduces Art. 4(1)(153A) defining vehicle financing arrangements for B31 retail sub-classification. Used in Art. 123(1)(d)(iii) for retail risk weights but definition not in glossary or specs. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 4(1)(153A)

- [ ] **D4.58** — **Art. 132(3A)/(3B) CIU country-of-establishment exposure notification undocumented.** PS1/26 Art. 132(3A)/(3B): institutions using look-through for CIU exposures must notify PRA if ≥2% of own funds exposed to CIUs established in third countries with deficient AML/CFT. Not in any spec file. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 132(3A)/(3B)

- [ ] **D4.59** — **Art. 139(2B) SA specialised lending exclusion from output floor undocumented.** PS1/26 Art. 139(2B): IRB firms using SA for specialised lending (Art. 122A) do not include those exposures in the output floor SA-RWA calculation. Not mentioned in `output-floor.md`. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 139(2B)

- [ ] **D4.60** — **Art. 143(7) overseas model approach grandfathering undocumented.** PS1/26 Art. 143(7): institutions may continue using IRB approaches previously approved by an overseas regulator, subject to PRA notification. Not documented in any spec or user guide. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 143(7)

- [ ] **D4.61** — **Art. 191A(4) unfunded credit protection covered by funded credit protection undocumented.** PS1/26 Art. 191A(4): where an unfunded credit protection provider is itself protected by funded credit protection, the institution may recognise the funded protection directly. Not in CRM docs. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 191A(4)

- [ ] **D4.62** — **Covered bond unrated derivation comment blurs CRR and B31.** `crr_risk_weights.py` comment on `covered_bond_unrated_derivation` dict says "CRR Art. 129(5), PRA PS1/26 Art. 129" but the 7 entries include B31 SCRA-derived values (30%, 40%, 75%) that cannot arise under CRR sovereign-derived approach. Doc references this dict without noting framework conflation. Overlaps D3.29 but this is the docs-side manifestation. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 129(5), PRA PS1/26 Art. 129

- [ ] **D4.63** — **Maturity mismatch adjustment formula attributed to Art. 238 throughout docs; actual formula is in Art. 239.** `crr/credit-risk-mitigation.md` (line 250), `basel31/credit-risk-mitigation.md` (line 381), `glossary.md` (line 238), `regulatory-compliance.md`, `plans/prd.md`, `features/index.md`, `user-guide/methodology/crm.md`, and `plans/implementation-plan.md` all cite "Art. 238" for the adjustment formula `(t − 0.25) / (T − 0.25)`. CRR Art. 238 only defines how to measure maturity (cap at 5 years, termination-option handling). The funded formula (C_VAM = C_VA × (t − t∗) / (T − t∗)) and unfunded formula (G_A = G∗ × (t − t∗) / (T − t∗)) are in **Art. 239** paragraphs 2 and 3. D4.38 (T without 5-year cap) is a different error in the same area. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 238 (maturity measurement), Art. 239(2)/(3) (adjustment formulas)

- [ ] **D4.64** — **CRR Art. 150(1) permanent partial use conditions not documented in any CRR spec.** `basel31/model-permissions.md` covers the Basel 3.1 Art. 150(1A) materiality thresholds, but no spec file documents the CRR Art. 150(1) conditions (a)-(j) for when a firm may apply SA permanently within an IRB framework (e.g., non-material counterparties, non-significant business units, UK government/BoE exposures, equity under government subsidy programmes). Art. 150(2) materiality thresholds (equity aggregate exceeds 10% of own funds on average, or 5% if fewer than 10 holdings) are also absent. These CRR conditions remain in force until end-2026 and govern current PPU decisions. **Effort: M** | Ref: CRR Art. 150(1)(a)-(j), Art. 150(2)

- [ ] **D4.65** — **CRR equity spec labels look-through/mandate-based approaches with B31 article numbers.** `crr/equity-approach.md` (lines 35, 103, 111, 131, 249) assigns "Art. 132A" to look-through and "Art. 132B" to mandate-based. In the historical UK CRR (before Art. 132 was omitted by SI 2021/1078), these were paragraphs within Art. 132 (para 4 = look-through, para 5 = mandate-based). Art. 132A and 132B are Basel 3.1 (PRA PS1/26) article numbers. The CRR section of the spec should reference "Art. 132(4)" and "Art. 132(5)" or note that Art. 132 was omitted. The B31 spec (`basel31/equity-approach.md`) correctly uses "Art. 132A(1)/Art. 152(4)" and "Art. 132A(2)/Art. 152(5)". **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 132(4)-(5) (pre-omission), PRA PS1/26 Art. 132A, Art. 132B

### New Phase 8 Findings — Comparison PDF, COREP/Pillar III, Code-Docs Alignment

- [ ] **D4.66** — **Art. 132(4A) CIU size-based PRA notification thresholds not documented.** PS1/26 Art. 132(4A): institutions must notify PRA when total RWA in relevant CIUs exceeds GBP 2 billion OR total exposure values in relevant CIUs exceed GBP 500 million. Must notify promptly and annually thereafter, including list of countries and exposure values per country. Distinct from D4.58 (Art. 132(3A)/(3B) — AML/CFT-based notification for ≥2% own funds in third-country CIUs). **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 132(4A)

- [ ] **D4.67** — **OF 07.00 granular risk weight row IDs not documented.** `output-reporting.md` and `reporting-differences.md` list "29 risk weight rows" and new percentage values but never document the COREP row IDs: 0171=15%, 0181=25%, 0182=30%, 0191=40%, 0192=45%, 0201=60%, 0202=65%, 0221=80%, 0222=85%, 0231=105%, 0232=110%, 0233=130%, 0234=135%, 0261=400% (replaces old 370% row). Any template implementation referencing these IDs has no spec. **Effort: S** | Ref: ps1-26-annex-ii-reporting-instructions.pdf pp. 95–96

- [ ] **D4.68** — **OF 07.00 RE sub-row hierarchy misstated.** `output-reporting.md` lists "Rows 0331–0344" but actual hierarchy from PDF is non-sequential: 0341 (not-dependent CRE), then 0343 (SME sub-row of 0341), then 0342 (dependent CRE), then 0344 (SME sub-row of 0342). Current doc doesn't clarify that 0343 is under 0341 and 0344 is under 0342. **Effort: S** | Ref: ps1-26-annex-ii-reporting-instructions.pdf pp. 90–91

- [ ] **D4.69** — **OF 08.01 col 0260 (post-adjustment RWEA) not named or defined.** PDF defines col 0260 = "Risk-Weighted Exposure Amount After Adjustments" as sum of 0251+0252+0253+0254. `output-reporting.md` field list jumps from col 0254 to col 0265 without documenting 0260. **Effort: S** | Ref: ps1-26-annex-ii-reporting-instructions.pdf p. 112

- [ ] **D4.70** — **OF 08.06 EL column references col 0282 (not pre-adjustment EL).** PDF says OF 08.06 col 0090 should follow "OFCR IRB 1 instructions for column 0282" (EL after post-model adjustments). `reporting-differences.md` says the EL column is "virtually identical" to CRR without noting this referential change to post-adjustment EL. **Effort: S** | Ref: ps1-26-annex-ii-reporting-instructions.pdf p. 129

- [ ] **D4.71** — **OF 08.07 row 0270 formula and col 0180 calculation not documented.** Row 0270 = "Percentage subject to permanent partial use (immateriality in aggregate)" with formula `sum(0110+0120)/(col_0060-col_0070)` for PPU threshold calculation. `reporting-differences.md` lists rows 0260/0270 as "Added" but doesn't document the formula. **Effort: S** | Ref: ps1-26-annex-ii-reporting-instructions.pdf pp. 135, 437

- [ ] **D4.72** — **UKB CR6 FIRB subclass asymmetry vs AIRB not documented.** `disclosure-differences.md` mentions F-IRB adds "financial corporates and large corporates" but PDF defines full FIRB CR6 subclass list: 1. Institutions, 2.1 SL, 2.2 Financial corporates/large corporates, 2.3 Other general corporates SME, 2.4 Other general corporates non-SME. The asymmetry between FIRB (4 corporate subclasses) and AIRB (different subclass structure) is not documented. **Effort: S** | Ref: Annex XXII pp. 7

- [ ] **D4.73** — **UKB CR7-A PDF col labelling typo should be flagged.** PDF Annex XXII (p. 14) defines col (o) for funded CP for slotting, then redefines col (n) for unfunded CP — should be col (p). `disclosure-differences.md` correctly shows o/p. Note the PDF typo to prevent implementors from following the PDF literally. **Effort: S** | Ref: Annex XXII p. 14

- [ ] **D4.74** — **ECA score lookup "not yet implemented" has no tracking item.** `crr/sa-risk-weights.md` (line 755) documents ECA-to-CQS mapping as a future enhancement with a "Not Yet Implemented" warning, but no corresponding item exists in DOCS_IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md or IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 136

- [ ] **D4.75** — **D3.6 scope incomplete: RE and other-physical ad-hoc haircuts also untraceable.** D3.6 tracks only the `receivables: Decimal("0.20")` ad-hoc approximation in `haircuts.py:71`. Same file (lines 68–72) also sets `real_estate: Decimal("0.00")` (zero haircut) and `other_physical: Decimal("0.40")` — also labelled "ad-hoc approximations" with no regulatory source cited. Art. 230 C*/C** threshold mechanism applies to non-financial collateral, not a flat haircut. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 230

### New Phase 18 Findings (2026-04-18) — Minor Fixes

- [ ] **D4.76** — **`crm.md` user-guide double-default section has ambiguous guarantor CQS threshold and omits A-IRB precondition.** `docs/user-guide/methodology/crm.md` lines 205–228 describe CRR double-default formula `K_dd = K_obligor × (0.15 + 160 × PD_guarantor)` and note B31 removal. Issues: (a) cites "Art. 153(3) paragraph 2" for the RW floor but Art. 153(3) para 2 is blanked under PS1/26 (which is correct for the B31 removal side but confusing for the CRR formula); (b) eligibility condition says guarantors must have "PD equivalent to CQS 2 or better (CQS 3 maintained threshold)" — ambiguous and inconsistent with CRR Art. 202 which references "CQS 3 or better"; (c) fails to note the A-IRB own-LGD precondition. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 153(3), Art. 202
- [ ] **D4.77** — **Art. 155(4) IMA floor condition and Art. 155(2) short-position netting rule absent from user-guide equity.** `docs/user-guide/methodology/equity.md` documents Art. 155 IRB Simple three risk weights (190%/290%/370%) but omits two material sub-rules documented in the CRR equity spec but absent from the user guide: (a) Art. 155(4) IMA approach — VaR-based floor requiring portfolio RWEA not below PD/LGD RWEA + EL×12.5; (b) Art. 155(2) short-position netting rule — short cash positions may offset long positions only if the hedge is explicit and covers at least 1 year. User guide is the primary practitioner reference. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 155(2), Art. 155(4)
- [~] **D4.78** — ~~**Art. 92(5) transitional opt-in notification and Art. 92(2D) sub-paragraphs not in output-floor spec.**~~ **PHASE 19 RE-VERIFICATION (2026-04-18): ALREADY FIXED.** `docs/specifications/basel31/output-floor.md` already contains the transitional schedule table, the entity-type carve-outs (b/c/d paragraphs), and the `skip_transitional` config note. Further Art. 92(2D)(b) sub-paragraph detail (separate reporting of floored TREA for sub-consolidated group) can be added as a minor polish but the material content is present. Closed. `docs/specifications/basel31/output-floor.md` states the Art. 92(5) transitional schedule is "permissive" ("may apply") and notes `skip_transitional` config flag but does not document: (a) formal PRA notification requirement for the election; (b) Art. 92(2D) condition — transitional floor application may only be made by a "CRR consolidation entity" or standalone institution (same entity-type gating as 92(2A)(a)); (c) Art. 92(2D)(b) requirement that when using transitional, floored TREA for the sub-consolidated group must be reported separately. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 92(5), Art. 92(2D); ps126app1.pdf p.15
- [ ] **D4.79** — **Art. 155(3) per-exposure RWEA+EL cap not in user-guide equity doc.** CRR Art. 155(3) requires that sum of EL×12.5 + RWEA for any individual equity exposure must not exceed EAD×12.5 (total capital cannot exceed 100% loss assumption for a single position). Stated in `crr/equity-approach.md` line 129 as a bullet but without distinct admonition/heading — easily overlooked. User-guide `equity.md` omits entirely. No code-docs note on whether calculator enforces this cap. **Effort: S** | Ref: CRR Art. 155(3)
- [ ] **D4.80** — **UKB CR5 B31 risk weight bucket list includes spurious 300% band.** `src/rwa_calc/reporting/pillar3/templates.py` line 236 includes `(3.00, "300%")` in `B31_CR5_RISK_WEIGHTS`. Basel 3.1 SA has no 300% RW — correct set goes 250% → 400% (the 400% IRB-transitional equity weight). Adjacent 250% and 400% bands are present; 300% is not a PRA PS1/26 SA weight. `pillar3-disclosures.md` col structure table and `disclosure-differences.md` do not list 300% either — confirmed code divergence from docs. Generates a column that will always be zero but is structurally erroneous. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 112, 122, 124, 133
- [ ] **D4.81** — **UKB OV1 pre-floor capital ratio rows (4a, 5a-b, 6a-b, 7a-b) missing from `pillar3-disclosures.md` and `templates.py`.** `disclosure-differences.md` (line 31, 61–62) lists UKB OV1 additional rows: "4a Total RWEAs (pre-floor)" and "5a-b, 6a-b, 7a-b Pre-floor capital ratios (CET1, Tier 1, Total)". Not listed in OV1 row structure table in `pillar3-disclosures.md` (shows only rows 1–5, 11–14, 24, 26, 27, 29). `B31_OV1_ROWS` in `templates.py` also omits them. Mandatory for output-floor-active institutions to allow market participants to see pre-floor capital position. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Annex XX
- [ ] **D4.82** — **UKB CR8 signed-movement convention absent from `pillar3-disclosures.md`.** `output-reporting.md` lines 217, 228 explicitly document CR8 RWEA flow rows 2–8 use signed values — decreases are negative. Convention is documented in spec but completely absent from `pillar3-disclosures.md` CR8 section, which only shows row structure without sign/convention note. Consumers generating templates will not know to negate decrease rows. Not in `disclosure-differences.md` either. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Annex XXII CR8 instructions
- [ ] **D4.83** — **UKB CMS1/CMS2 col d GCRA reconciliation link absent.** `pillar3-disclosures.md` documents CMS1 col d as "RWA calculated using full standardised approach" but neither CMS1 nor CMS2 sections mention the OF-ADJ / GCRA reconciliation: col d is the S-TREA input **before** the OF-ADJ is applied (matches OF 02.01 col 0040). Relationship between CMS1 col d, OF 02.01 col 0040, and OF-ADJ formula `12.5 × (IRB_T2 – IRB_CET1 – GCRA + SA_T2)` is entirely absent. Important because GCRA is capped at 1.25% of S-TREA (Art. 62(c), Art. 92(2A)), meaning S-TREA reported in CMS1 directly gates GCRA T2 capacity. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 62(c), Art. 92(2A)
- [ ] **D4.84** — **UKB CR9 F-IRB class breakdown doesn't match CR6 (missing financial/large corporates row).** `pillar3-disclosures.md` CR9 section F-IRB breakdown (lines 602–610) lists institutions, corporates (with SL), and "other general corporates (SME/non-SME)" but omits the "financial corporates and large corporates" row. `templates.py` `CR9_FIRB_CLASSES` (lines 574–580) has `corporate_sme` but no separate "financial corporates and large corporates" class matching what CR6 F-IRB describes. CR6 section (lines 337–343) correctly lists this as a key F-IRB addition. CR9 should align and note it follows the same F-IRB class breakdown as CR6. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Annex XXII paras 12–15
