---

## Notes

- Equity haircut values (20%/30%) confirmed correct against PRA PS1/26 Art. 224 Table 3 (10-day liquidation period). BCBS CRE22.53 values are 25%/35% — skill references used BCBS values in error.
- Corporate CQS 5 = 150% confirmed from PRA PS1/26 Art. 122 Table 6. BCBS CRE20.42 reduced to 100% but PRA did not adopt.
- Equity transitional rule numbering (D2.25/D4.16): Rule 4.1 = scope restriction (firms without IRB permission at 31 Dec 2026), Rule 4.2 = standard schedule (160%→250%), Rule 4.3 = higher-risk schedule (220%→400%). Rule 4.1 is NOT a schedule — earlier docs that labelled the scope restriction as "Rule 4.1(a)/(b)/(c)" or listed schedules as "Rules 4.1/4.2" were incorrect. IRB firms follow Rules 4.4-4.6 (bifurcated portfolio: SA equities at 31 Dec 2026 use Rules 4.2/4.3 schedule; IRB equities at 31 Dec 2026 use higher of legacy IRB RW vs transitional SA RW).
- PRA output floor transitional schedule: 4-year (60/65/70/72.5%, 2027-2030), not BCBS 6-year.
- PRA slotting pre-op PF: no separate table (uses standard non-HVCRE), not BCBS CRE33 elevated weights.
- Cross-references to `IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md` items noted where doc issues overlap with code issues (P4.x series).
- PRA deviation from BCBS on CRE income-producing: PRA Art. 124I uses <=80%: 100%, >80%: 110%. BCBS uses <=60%: 70%, >60%-80%: 90%, >80%: 110%.
- PRA covered bond rated risk weights (D4.20): PRA PS1/26 Art. 129(4) Table 7 is **identical to CRR Table 6A** (10/20/20/50/50/100%). BCBS CRE20.28-29 reduced CQS 2 to 15% and collapsed CQS 4-6 to 50% — PRA did not adopt. The only B31 change is to Art. 129(5) unrated derivation (expanded from 4 to 7 entries for new institution RWs). Code bug D3.21 uses BCBS values.
- Large FSE threshold for FI scalar: PRA PS1/26 Art. 1.3 defines "large FSE" as total assets > GBP 79bn (CRR Art. 4(1)(146) = EUR 70bn). This is entirely distinct from Art. 147A large corporate revenue threshold of GBP 440m.
- Art. 128 (high-risk 150%) is confirmed active in PRA PS1/26 (page 59, paras 1 and 3); para 2 left blank. **Under current UK CRR (pre-2027), Art. 128 was omitted by SI 2021/1078 effective 1 Jan 2022** — the high-risk class is dead letter until Basel 3.1 reintroduces it.
- CRR Art. 161(1)(d) = covered bond LGD 11.25% (permissive — "may be assigned"). Art. 161(1)(d) is NOT financial collateral. Financial collateral 0% LGDS is Art. 230 Table 5. Several doc tables previously cited "Art. 161(1)(d)" for financial collateral — corrected in D3.3.
- Art. 132 (CIU) omitted from UK CRR by SI 2021/1078 (1 Jan 2022), moved to PRA Rulebook (CRR Part). **D1.20 RESOLVED:** CRR2 (Regulation 2019/876) set Art. 132(2) fallback to **1,250%**. PRA PS1/26 Art. 132(2) confirms 1,250% (PDF page 62: "shall assign a risk weight of 1,250% ('fall-back approach')"). The original D1.20 claim that CRR fallback was 100% was pre-CRR2. Code bug filed as D3.15: code uses 150%/250%/400% (Art. 133 equity weights) instead of 1,250% (Art. 132(2) CIU fallback). The distinction is: Art. 132(2) = true fallback (1,250%); Art. 132B(2) = exclusion treatment reclassifying CIU holdings as equity under Art. 133.
- **D1.30 RESOLVED:** CRR institution CQS 2 = **50%** (UK onshored CRR Art. 120 Table 3, crr.pdf p.119). Basel 3.1 ECRA = **30%** (PRA PS1/26 Art. 120 Table 3, ps126app1.pdf p.40). The 30% is a deliberate Basel 3.1 change that introduces a new intermediate band for well-rated (A-range) institutions. No PRA Rulebook overlay or supervisory statement was identified that reduces CRR CQS 2 below 50%. Code bug filed as D3.17. MDB Table 2B CQS 2 = 30% in code may have the same misattribution — flagged for verification in D3.17.
- Art. 124A qualifying criteria: **6 top-level criteria** (a)-(f) at para 1, not 9. Sub-conditions and paras 2-4 expand detail but the primary structure is 6 named criteria.
- **CRR2 payroll/pension 35%:** Regulation (EU) 2019/876 amendment F68 inserted a second subparagraph in CRR Art. 123 assigning 35% risk weight to payroll/pension-secured loans, subject to 4 conditions (unconditional deduction, insurance, ≤20% aggregate, ≤10yr maturity). PRA PS1/26 Art. 123(4) preserves this verbatim — the PS1/26 note explicitly states "This rule and Article 123A correspond to Article 123 of CRR as it applied immediately before revocation by the Treasury." The code implements this only for Basel 3.1 (`B31_RETAIL_PAYROLL_LOAN_RW`); CRR path applies flat 75% to all retail. Code Art. references cite Art. 123(3)(a-b) which is wrong — Art. 123(3) covers the three-tier risk weight structure (45%/75%/100%); the payroll/pension treatment is Art. 123(4).
- Art. 155 (IRB Simple equity) has exactly three categories: exchange-traded (290%), PE diversified (190%), all other (370%). No "government-supported" category exists anywhere in the CRR or Basel 3.1 text.
- **Art. 158 (expected loss)** omitted from UK CRR by SI 2021/1078, reg. 6(3)(e) (1 Jan 2022). EL rules moved to PRA Rulebook (CRR Firms). PS1/26 reinstates Art. 158 with modifications (new para 6A for EL monotonicity). **Art. 159 (EL vs provisions comparison) was NOT omitted** — retained in UK CRR as substituted by EU 2019/630. Art. 152 (IRB CIU treatment) also omitted by same SI, reg. 6(3)(d).
- D4.8 flagged for review: CQS 4 govt bond haircut row appears present in current version of `credit-risk-mitigation.md`.
- Phase 3 PDF verification confirmed all 27 existing D1.x items and all 31 existing D2.x items. 4 new P1 items, 2 new P3 items, and 4 new P4 items added based on CRR omission findings and threshold clarifications.
- D1.16 re-check: `slotting-changes.md` shows 80/100/120/350% for pre-op PF. These values match the PRA B31 standard non-HVCRE table — the error is that PRA has NO separate pre-op table, so showing any pre-op-specific table is misleading (the same weights apply to all PF). Needs further verification whether the skill file should remove the pre-op section entirely or note that pre-op uses standard weights.
- D1.13-D1.19 skill file fixes are BLOCKED by sandbox write permissions on `.claude/skills/`. User must fix manually or adjust sandbox policy. All errors verified correct as documented.
- CRR institution tables: CRR has exactly 3 institution tables — Table 3 (Art. 120(1), rated long-term), Table 4 (Art. 120(2), rated short-term), Table 5 (Art. 121(1), unrated sovereign-derived). There is **no Table 4A** in the CRR. Both Tables 3 and 4 use the institution's own ECAI rating. Basel 3.1 introduces Table 4A (Art. 120(2B)) for short-term ECAI assessments.
- B31 ECRA short-term Table 4 code bug: `B31_ECRA_SHORT_TERM_RISK_WEIGHTS` in `b31_risk_weights.py` has CQS 4-5 at 20% — should be 50% per PRA PS1/26 Art. 120(2). Filed as D3.14.
- PRA PS1/26 Art. 111 Table A1 has **7 rows** (not 6). Rows 3 and 4 are separate (both 50%): Row 3 = other issued OBS items (not credit substitutes); Row 4 = (a) NIFs/RUFs, (b) UK residential mortgage commitments. The Row 4(b) mortgage carve-out is PRA-specific (not in BCBS CRE20.93–98, where mortgage commitments would fall into "any other commitment" at 40%). CRR Annex I (pages 434-435) has no corresponding separate mortgage category. Row 6 = medium/low-risk issued items (documentary credits, warranties, bonds, guarantees) at 20%. Row 7 = unconditionally cancellable at 10%.
- **Art. 127 provision threshold denominator (D4.32/D3.19):** CRR Art. 127(1) (crr.pdf pp. 126-127) uses "the unsecured part of the exposure value if those specific credit risk adjustments and deductions were not applied" — the pre-provision unsecured value. PRA PS1/26 Art. 127(1) (ps126app1.pdf p. 59) uses "the outstanding amount of the item or facility" — the gross outstanding balance (full facility, not just unsecured). The denominators are meaningfully different: CRR = pre-provision unsecured; PRA = gross outstanding. CRR code path correctly reconstructs pre-provision unsecured via `(ead + provision_deducted) × unsecured_pct`. B31 code path incorrectly uses `unsecured_ead` instead of gross outstanding — filed as D3.19.
- **D2.15/D2.16 fix notes:** `output-floor.md` had two errors: (1) OF-ADJ formula was `max(0, SA_T2 - IRB_T2 + GCRA + IRB_CET1)` — all signs inverted and wrapped in max(0,...) that doesn't exist in the regulation. Correct formula per Art. 92(2A) page 13: `12.5 × (IRB_T2 – IRB_CET1 – GCRA + SA_T2)` (matches `output-reporting.md` and code `_floor.py:56`). (2) Entity carve-out paras described "investment firms", "CCPs", "no-IRB-permission firms" — entirely fabricated. Actual paras: (b) non-ring-fenced on sub-consolidated, (c) ring-fenced at individual (when in sub-consolidation group), (d) international subsidiaries on consolidated. Matches `output-reporting.md:49` and code `config.py:340-361`.
- **Phase 8 — comparison-of-the-final-rules.pdf** is a 502-page PS9/24 near-final → PS1/26 final comparison (NOT a CRR↔B31 comparison). Changes are small final tweaks. Most material CRR→B31 changes are unchanged between near-final and final. PDF is text-extractable via PyMuPDF.
- **Phase 8 — CRR Art. 120(2) Table 4 short-term institution gap:** CRR SA calculator branch has NO short-term institution preferential treatment. Rated institutions with ≤3m residual maturity should get CQS 1–3 = 20%, CQS 4–5 = 50%, CQS 6 = 150% (Art. 120(2) Table 4). CQS 4–5 are overstated at 100% (standard Table 3 values). B31 branch correctly implements this at lines 726–748. CRR branch has analogous PSE short-term check but no institution equivalent. Filed as D2.57.
- **Phase 8 — Art. 129(1B) covered bond CQS 2 concentration permission:** Entirely new in final PS1/26 (absent from PS9/24 near-final). Allows PRA permission for CQS 2 on up to 10% of outstanding covered bonds where CQS 1 creates UK concentration problems. Filed as D3.30.
- **Phase 8 — Subordinated LGDS code gap:** `crr/credit-risk-mitigation.md` correctly flags subordinated LGDS values (receivables 65%, RE 65%, other physical 70%) as "Not Yet Implemented" (from D3.10 docs fix). The engine uses single LGDS regardless of subordination status. Code fix not yet tracked in IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md — doc side already complete.

Phase 19 adds 14 new items (D1.48 P1 / D2.69 P2 / D3.50–D3.56 P3 / D4.85–D4.90 P4) and records 2 corrections to Phase 18 items (D1.47 INACCURATE, D4.78 ALREADY-FIXED). See corrections inline at the original item entries above.

### New Phase 19 Findings (2026-04-18) — Regulatory / Coverage Gaps

- [x] **D1.48** — ~~**GCRA Art. 62(c) qualifying-criteria definition absent from output-floor spec.**~~ **FIXED:** Added comprehensive "General Credit Risk Adjustments (GCRA) — Qualifying Criteria" section to `docs/specifications/basel31/output-floor.md` between OF-ADJ Capital Adjustment and Entity-Type Applicability covering all four D1.48 gaps: (a) GCRA vs SCRA definition table sourced from Commission Delegated Regulation (EU) No 183/2014 Art. 1(5)(a)/(b) with "freely and fully available" language verbatim, noting Reg 183/2014 superseded EBA GL 2013/04; (b) IFRS 9 Stage 1/2/3 mapping table with explicit note that Stage 2 is the ambiguous bucket (collective → GCRA; individual watch-list → SCRA); (c) exclusion admonition for "funds for general banking risk" (Art. 110(2) final sentence verbatim); (d) Framework Treatment by Approach table showing SA GCRA → Art. 62(c) `SA_T2`, IRB GCRA → Art. 159 Pool B, SA SCRA non-defaulted → EAD reduction per Art. 111(1)(a), IRB SCRA → Pool B/D; (e) Mixed-Approach Allocation (Art. 110(3)(a)–(c) and Art. 110(3A) RW Substitution); (f) Double-Count Avoidance invariants covering EAD/T2 exclusivity, securitisation exclusion (Art. 159(2)(b)), Risk-Weight Substitution exclusion (Art. 159(2)(c)); (g) Input Source and Validation subsection mapping inputs to `OutputFloorConfig.gcra_amount` / `OutputFloorConfig.sa_t2_credit` with CalculationConfig factory example. Verbatim regulatory text extracted to `tmp/gcra_regulatory_extract.md` (Art. 62(2A) p.13, Art. 110 pp.19-20, Art. 111(1)(a) p.29, Art. 159 pp.108-109). - [ ] **D2.69** — **User-guide exposure-class pages missing for real-estate (loan-splitting), CIUs, and covered bonds.** `docs/user-guide/exposure-classes/` contains only 6 files: `index.md`, `central-govt-central-bank.md`, `institution.md`, `corporate.md`, `retail.md`, `other.md`. Three material SA exposure classes have no dedicated page: (a) **secured-by-real-estate** — Art. 124A–124L loan-splitting mechanics (hard-test/soft-test, RE/non-RE carve, LTV banding, income-producing vs owner-occupied, Art. 124K ADC treatment) currently scattered across `methodology/standardised-approach.md` and specs; (b) **CIUs** — Art. 132/132a look-through, mandate-based, and fallback approaches; (c) **covered bonds** — Art. 129 eligibility, Art. 129(1B) concentration carve-out, preferential weighting. These are practitioner-facing pages — operational teams have no user-guide entry point. **Effort: L** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 124A–L, 132/132a, 129; covers D2.34, D2.66 partially

### New Phase 19 Findings (2026-04-18) — Code-Docs Alignment

- [ ] **D3.50** — **P19-01: `enable_double_default` config knob absent from configuration docs.** `src/rwa_calc/contracts/config.py` line 819 defines `enable_double_default: bool = False` on `IRBPermissions`. CRR Art. 153(3)/(202) double-default is documented regulatorily in `user-guide/methodology/crm.md` and `crr/credit-risk-mitigation.md` but the **config knob** to enable it is not in `docs/api/configuration.md`, `docs/configuration.md`, or the factory-method documentation for `CalculationConfig.crr()`. Default `False` means no practitioner turns it on without knowing the knob exists. **Effort: S** | Ref: `contracts/config.py:819`

- [ ] **D3.51** — **P19-02: `use_investment_grade_assessment` config knob absent from docs.** `config.py` line 820 defines `use_investment_grade_assessment: bool = False` controlling whether the Art. 153(3) investment-grade assessment path (CRR) is applied. Not documented in `api/configuration.md` or IRB spec files. Default `False` disables a CRR regulatory option that some practitioners may need. **Effort: S** | Ref: `contracts/config.py:820`

- [ ] **D3.52** — **P19-03: `crm_collateral_method` / `airb_collateral_method` enums absent from configuration docs.** `config.py` lines 825, 830 expose `CRMCollateralMethod` (simple / fcsm / fccm) and `AIRBCollateralMethod` (simple / effective-lgd) enums on `CalculationConfig`. Not referenced in `docs/api/configuration.md`, `docs/configuration.md`, or `glossary.md`. `domain/enums.py` defines both but the docs entry points don't show them as tunable knobs. **Effort: S** | Ref: `contracts/config.py:825,830`; `domain/enums.py`

- [ ] **D3.53** — **P19-04: `life_ins_collateral_value` / `life_ins_secured_rw` output columns absent from output-schemas.** `src/rwa_calc/engine/crm/life_insurance.py` produces `life_ins_collateral_value` and `life_ins_secured_rw` columns but `docs/data-model/output-schemas.md` (Phase 18 partial coverage) omits both. Art. 212(2) life insurance collateral is a distinct CRM path with its own preferential RW mechanic. **Effort: S** | Ref: `engine/crm/life_insurance.py`; PRA PS1/26 Art. 212(2)

- [ ] **D3.54** — **P19-05: `supporting_factor_applied` column name mismatch (docs vs source).** Source (`engine/sa/supporting_factors.py`, `aggregator/_supporting_factors.py`) emits the column as `supporting_factor_applied`. `docs/data-model/output-schemas.md` and `docs/specifications/output-reporting.md` refer to it as `sme_supporting_factor_applied` (legacy name). Rename pre-dates the infrastructure supporting factor — current column is generic. **Effort: S** | Ref: `engine/sa/supporting_factors.py`; `aggregator/_supporting_factors.py`

- [ ] **D3.55** — **P19-06: CLS004, CLS005, IRB006, SA005, SF001 error codes undocumented.** `src/rwa_calc/contracts/errors.py` defines CLS004, CLS005, IRB006, SA005, SF001 but they are not re-exported from `contracts/__init__.py` and not listed in `docs/api/error-codes.md` / `docs/error-codes.md`. Phase 18 D3.48 tracks `hierarchy.py`-only codes; this is the complementary set for classifier/IRB/SA/supporting-factors. **Effort: S** | Ref: `contracts/errors.py`

- [ ] **D3.57** — **SCRA Art. 121(4) 6m trade-finance extension missing from code branch.** `src/rwa_calc/engine/sa/namespace.py:420` gates the SCRA short-term unrated-institution branch on `original_mty <= 0.25` (3m) only — the symmetric Art. 121(4) `is_short_term_trade_lc & (original_mty <= 0.5)` extension applied on the ECRA branch at lines 401-408 is not replicated. Consequence: a 5-month USD documentary credit to an unrated Grade A institution arising from goods movement receives the standard Grade A 40% weight instead of the Table 5A 20% short-term weight. B31 spec (`specifications/basel31/sa-risk-weights.md` "SCRA Short-Term Trade Finance Exception (Art. 121(4))") correctly documents the 6-month eligibility — the gap is code-only. Discovered during D2.41 closure 2026-04-21. **Effort: S** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 121(4); `engine/sa/namespace.py:420`

- [ ] **D3.59** — **Art. 124(4) mixed RE split not implementable under current input schema.** Discovered during D2.42 closure (2026-04-22). PRA PS1/26 Art. 124(4) requires a single RE exposure secured by both residential and commercial property to be split proportionally by property value, with each part routed through its own risk-weight article (Art. 124F–I if both parts separately qualify under Art. 124A; Art. 124J on both parts otherwise). The current input schema in `src/rwa_calc/data/schemas.py` exposes a single `property_value` and `property_type` per exposure row, making the proportional split impossible in-engine — firms must currently pre-split mixed-use exposures into two input rows at the loader boundary (documented as a workaround in the new B31 SA spec Art. 124 section). To implement Art. 124(4) natively the schema needs either (a) new optional fields `residential_property_value` / `commercial_property_value` on Loan / Contingent with a dedicated `is_mixed_re` Boolean flag, or (b) a repeated-collateral structure allowing N property rows per exposure. The B31 SA calculator branch in `src/rwa_calc/engine/sa/namespace.py` then needs an `is_mixed_re` fan-out path that computes per-component EAD and applies the Art. 124A gate to each component's qualifying status separately (Art. 124J is the default; Art. 124F–I applies only when both parts qualify). Spec-side now complete at `docs/specifications/basel31/sa-risk-weights.md#real-estate--framework-scope-art-124`. **Effort: M** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 124(4); `src/rwa_calc/data/schemas.py`; `src/rwa_calc/engine/sa/namespace.py`

- [ ] **D3.60** — **Art. 138(1)(g) implicit-support prohibition and Art. 139(6) higher-of rule not implemented — input-schema gap.** The facility schema exposes a single `external_cqs` (post Art. 138 resolution) with no field distinguishing **issue-specific** from **general issuer** ratings (prerequisite for Art. 139(6)(b)), and no field flagging whether an ECAI assessment **incorporates implicit government support** (prerequisite for Art. 138(1)(g) suppression and the Art. 139(6) clean-vs-with-support comparison). As a result, every rated institution exposure is treated as if the rating complies with Art. 138(1)(g); no higher-of uplift is applied. Firms with material rated-institution portfolios whose ratings embed implicit sovereign support must either (a) pre-adjust `external_cqs` offline or (b) set `due_diligence_override_rw` via the Art. 110A pathway. New input fields required: `rating_is_issue_specific: Bool` and `rating_incorporates_implicit_support: Bool` (or equivalent multi-rating structure). Related to D2.49 (documentation closure). **Effort: M** | Ref: PRA PS1/26 Art. 138(1)(g), Art. 139(6); `src/rwa_calc/data/schemas.py`, `src/rwa_calc/engine/hierarchy.py:284-328`, `src/rwa_calc/engine/sa/calculator.py`

- [ ] **D3.58** — **LFSE article citation wrong in code + B31 GBP 79bn threshold not in code.** Two code-side findings from D1.49 closure (2026-04-21). (a) `src/rwa_calc/contracts/config.py:586` comment `# EUR 70bn — CRR Art. 4(1)(146)` and line 600 docstring `Art. 4(1)(146)` both cite the wrong CRR article — Art. 4(1)(146) is the "large institution" G-SII/O-SII definition, not the LFSE definition. Correct citation is **CRR Art. 142(1)(4)** (EUR 70bn) / **PS1/26 Glossary p. 78** (GBP 79bn). (b) `RegulatoryThresholds.basel_3_1()` hardcodes `lfse_total_assets_threshold=Decimal("0")` with comment "Not applicable under Basel 3.1" — but under Basel 3.1 the threshold IS applicable (PS1/26 Glossary defines LFSE at GBP 79 billion). The engine relies solely on the upstream `apply_fi_scalar` flag, so the missing threshold has no runtime effect today, but any downstream code that reads the config field will see 0 instead of the correct GBP 79 billion. Recommend: (i) update comments to cite Art. 142(1)(4); (ii) replace `Decimal("0")` with `Decimal("79000000000")` (or rename the field to indicate it is informational only under the current flag-driven design). **Effort: S** | Ref: `src/rwa_calc/contracts/config.py:586,600,652`; PS1/26 Glossary p. 78; CRR Art. 142(1)(4)

- [ ] **D3.56** — **P19-07: CRE22.70–85 IRB guarantee parameter-substitution steps missing from B31 CRM spec.** `src/rwa_calc/engine/irb/guarantee.py` implements the CRE22.70–85 (BCBS) / PRA PS1/26 Art. 161/201/202/236 parameter-substitution path for IRB guarantees (PD substitution, LGD adjustment, correlation re-derivation, and Art. 236A maturity adjustment). `docs/specifications/basel31/credit-risk-mitigation.md` covers guarantee haircuts and eligibility but does not document the **IRB-specific substitution steps**: (a) PD substitution (CRE22.72), (b) LGD adjustment based on guarantor seniority (CRE22.73), (c) recalculation of correlation (CRE22.74), (d) maturity adjustment treatment (CRE22.80). Substantive spec gap. **Effort: M** | Ref: `engine/irb/guarantee.py`; PRA PS1/26 Art. 202, 236; BCBS CRE22.70–85

- [ ] **D4.89** — **Config factory methods (`.crr()` / `.basel_3_1()`) lack worked parameter-override example in docs.** `CalculationConfig.crr()` and `.basel_3_1()` accept keyword overrides (e.g. `airb_collateral_method=AIRBCollateralMethod.EFFECTIVE_LGD`) but `docs/api/configuration.md` shows only the defaults, no override example.
